(*
In this file, we provide a builder to construct a symmetric displayed monoidal category on a locally propositional displayed category [make_symmetric_monoidal_disp_cat_locally_prop].

This builder takes into account the symmetric aspects found in a monoidal category,
e.g., the (displayed) right unitor can be constructed from the left unitor (provided a braiding); the assumptions on the right unitor, follow from those on the left unitor.
*)

Require Import UniMath.Foundations.All.

Section Construct_SymmetricMonoidal_On_LocallyProp_DisplayedCategories.

  Context (V : sym_monoidal_cat) (D : disp_cat V).

  Context (disp_tensor_ob : ∏ x y : V, D x → D y → D (x ⊗ y)).
  Let T {x y : V} (xx : D x) (yy : D y) : D (x ⊗ y) := disp_tensor_ob _ _ xx yy.

  Context (disp_lwhisker : ∏ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V⟦ y1, y2 ⟧) (xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) (yy2 : D y2),
              yy1 -->[ g] yy2 → T xx yy1 -->[ x ⊗^{V}_{l} g] T xx yy2).
  Let Tl
    {x y1 y2 : V} {g : V⟦ y1, y2 ⟧} (xx : D x) {yy1 : D y1} {yy2 : D y2}
    (gg : yy1 -->[ g] yy2)
    : T xx yy1 -->[ x ⊗^{V}_{l} g] T xx yy2
    := disp_lwhisker _ _ _ _ _ _ _ gg.

  Context (disp_braiding : ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) (yy : D y), T xx yy -->[sym_mon_braiding V x y] T yy xx).
  Let B {x y : V} (xx : D x) (yy : D y)
    : T xx yy -->[sym_mon_braiding V x y] T yy xx
    := disp_braiding x y xx yy.

  
V: sym_monoidal_cat
D: disp_cat V
disp_tensor_ob: ∏ x y : V, D x → D y → D (x ⊗ y)
T:= λ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y), disp_tensor_ob x y xx yy: ∏ x y : V, D x → D y → D (x ⊗ y)
disp_lwhisker: ∏ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧)
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
(yy2 : D y2),
yy1 -->[ g] yy2
→ T xx yy1 -->[
  x ⊗^{ V}_{l} g] T xx yy2
Tl:= λ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧) 
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
(yy2 : D y2) (gg : yy1 -->[ g] yy2),
disp_lwhisker x y1 y2 g xx yy1 yy2 gg: ∏ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧) 
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
(yy2 : D y2),
yy1 -->[ g] yy2
→ T xx yy1 -->[ x ⊗^{ V}_{l} g] T xx yy2
disp_braiding: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
T xx yy -->[
sym_mon_braiding V x y] 
T yy xx
B:= λ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y), disp_braiding x y xx yy: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
T xx yy -->[ sym_mon_braiding V x y] T yy xx
x1, x2, y: V
f: V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧
xx1: D x1
xx2: D x2
yy: D y
ff: xx1 -->[ f] xx2
T xx1 yy -->[ f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y] T xx2 yy

T xx2 yy
f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y · V x2 y · sym_mon_braiding V y x2 =
f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y

V: sym_monoidal_cat
D: disp_cat V
disp_tensor_ob: ∏ x y : V, D x → D y → D (x ⊗ y)
T:= λ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y), disp_tensor_ob x y xx yy: ∏ x y : V, D x → D y → D (x ⊗ y)
disp_lwhisker: ∏ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧)
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
(yy2 : D y2),
yy1 -->[ g] yy2
→ T xx yy1 -->[
  x ⊗^{ V}_{l} g] T xx yy2
Tl:= λ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧)

        (identity x)) ((pr12 V) y x) @
   assoc' (identity x ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x y)
     ((pr12 V) y x) @
   maponpaths (compose (identity x ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
     (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x y)) @
   id_right (identity x ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
  (B xx yy ;; Tl yy (id_disp xx) ;; B yy xx) =
transportb (mor_disp (T xx yy) (T xx yy))
  (bifunctor_rightid V y x) (id_disp (T xx yy))


    
V: sym_monoidal_cat
D: disp_cat V
disp_tensor_ob: ∏ x y : V, D x → D y → D (x ⊗ y)
T:= λ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y), disp_tensor_ob x y xx yy: ∏ x y : V, D x → D y → D (x ⊗ y)
disp_lwhisker: ∏ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧)
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
(yy2 : D y2),
yy1 -->[ g] yy2
→ T xx yy1 -->[
  x ⊗^{ V}_{l} g] T xx yy2
Tl:= λ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧) 
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
(yy2 : D y2) (gg : yy1 -->[ g] yy2),
disp_lwhisker x y1 y2 g xx yy1 yy2 gg: ∏ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧) 
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
(yy2 : D y2),
yy1 -->[ g] yy2
→ T xx yy1 -->[ x ⊗^{ V}_{l} g] T xx yy2
disp_braiding: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
T xx yy -->[
sym_mon_braiding V x y] 
T yy xx
B:= λ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y), disp_braiding x y xx yy: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
T xx yy -->[ sym_mon_braiding V x y] T yy xx
Tr:= λ (x1 x2 y : V) (f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧) 
(xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2) 
(yy : D y) (ff : xx1 -->[ f] xx2),
let t := B xx1 yy ;; Tl yy ff ;; B yy xx2 in
transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx2 yy))
  (maponpaths_2 compose
     (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1 x2 y
        f) (sym_mon_braiding V y x2) @
   assoc' (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) 
     (V x2 y) (sym_mon_braiding V y x2) @
   maponpaths (compose (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
     (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x2 y)) @
   id_right (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) t: ∏ (x1 x2 y : V) (f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧) 
(xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2) 
(yy : D y),
xx1 -->[ f] xx2
→ T xx1 yy -->[ f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y] T xx2 yy
disp_lwhisker_preserves_id: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x)
(yy : D y),
Tl xx (id_disp yy) =
transportb
  (mor_disp (T xx yy)
     (T xx yy))
  (bifunctor_leftid V x y)
  (id_disp (T xx yy))
B_inv: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
B xx yy ;; B yy xx =
transportb (mor_disp (T xx yy) (T xx yy))
  (sym_mon_braiding_inv V x y)
  (id_disp (T xx yy))
x, y: V
xx: D x
yy: D y
transportf (mor_disp (T xx yy) (T xx yy))
  (maponpaths_2 compose
     (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x x y
        (identity x)) ((pr12 V) y x) @
   assoc' (identity x ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x y)
     ((pr12 V) y x) @
   maponpaths (compose (identity x ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
     (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x y)) @
   id_right (identity x ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
  (B xx yy ;; Tl yy (id_disp xx) ;; B yy xx) = ?b

  (bifunctor_leftid V x y)
  (id_disp (T xx yy))
B_inv: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
B xx yy ;; B yy xx =
transportb (mor_disp (T xx yy) (T xx yy))
  (sym_mon_braiding_inv V x y)
  (id_disp (T xx yy))
x, y: V
xx: D x
yy: D y
transportf (mor_disp (T xx yy) (T xx yy))
  (maponpaths_2 compose
     (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x x y
        (identity x)) ((pr12 V) y x) @
   assoc' (identity x ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x y)
     ((pr12 V) y x) @
   maponpaths (compose (identity x ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
     (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x y)) @
   id_right (identity x ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
  (B xx yy ;; transportb
                (mor_disp (T yy xx) (T yy xx))
                (bifunctor_leftid V y x)
                (id_disp (T yy xx)) ;; B yy xx) =
transportb (mor_disp (T xx yy) (T xx yy))
  (bifunctor_rightid V y x) (id_disp (T xx yy))

   maponpaths (compose (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
     (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x2 y)) @
   id_right (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) t: ∏ (x1 x2 y : V) (f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧) 
(xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2) 
(yy : D y),
xx1 -->[ f] xx2
→ T xx1 yy -->[ f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y] T xx2 yy
disp_lwhisker_preserves_id: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x)
(yy : D y),
Tl xx (id_disp yy) =
transportb
  (mor_disp (T xx yy)
     (T xx yy))
  (bifunctor_leftid V x y)
  (id_disp (T xx yy))
B_inv: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
B xx yy ;; B yy xx =
transportb (mor_disp (T xx yy) (T xx yy))
  (sym_mon_braiding_inv V x y)
  (id_disp (T xx yy))
x, y: V
xx: D x
yy: D y
transportf (mor_disp (T xx yy) (T xx yy))
  (cancel_postcomposition
     ((pr12 V) x y · identity (y ⊗_{ V} x))
     ((pr12 V) x y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} identity x)
     ((pr12 V) y x)
     (maponpaths (compose ((pr12 V) x y))
        (! bifunctor_leftid V y x)) @
   maponpaths_2 compose
     (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x x y
        (identity x)) ((pr12 V) y x) @
   assoc' (identity x ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x y)
     ((pr12 V) y x) @
   maponpaths (compose (identity x ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
     (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x y)) @
   id_right (identity x ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
  (transportf (mor_disp (T xx yy) (T yy xx))
     (! id_right ((pr12 V) x y)) (B xx yy) ;; B yy xx) =
transportf (mor_disp (T xx yy) (T xx yy))
  (! bifunctor_rightid V y x) (id_disp (T xx yy))

  (! bifunctor_rightid V y x) (id_disp (T xx yy))

    
V: sym_monoidal_cat
D: disp_cat V
disp_tensor_ob: ∏ x y : V, D x → D y → D (x ⊗ y)
T:= λ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y), disp_tensor_ob x y xx yy: ∏ x y : V, D x → D y → D (x ⊗ y)
disp_lwhisker: ∏ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧)
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
(yy2 : D y2),
yy1 -->[ g] yy2
→ T xx yy1 -->[
  x ⊗^{ V}_{l} g] T xx yy2
Tl:= λ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧) 
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
(yy2 : D y2) (gg : yy1 -->[ g] yy2),
disp_lwhisker x y1 y2 g xx yy1 yy2 gg: ∏ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧) 
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
(yy2 : D y2),
yy1 -->[ g] yy2
→ T xx yy1 -->[ x ⊗^{ V}_{l} g] T xx yy2
disp_braiding: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
T xx yy -->[
sym_mon_braiding V x y] 
T yy xx
B:= λ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y), disp_braiding x y xx yy: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
T xx yy -->[ sym_mon_braiding V x y] T yy xx
Tr:= λ (x1 x2 y : V) (f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧) 
(xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2) 
(yy : D y) (ff : xx1 -->[ f] xx2),
let t := B xx1 yy ;; Tl yy ff ;; B yy xx2 in
transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx2 yy))
  (maponpaths_2 compose
     (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1 x2 y
        f) (sym_mon_braiding V y x2) @
   assoc' (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) 
     (V x2 y) (sym_mon_braiding V y x2) @
   maponpaths (compose (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
     (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x2 y)) @
   id_right (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) t: ∏ (x1 x2 y : V) (f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧) 
(xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2) 
(yy : D y),
xx1 -->[ f] xx2
→ T xx1 yy -->[ f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y] T xx2 yy
disp_lwhisker_preserves_id: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x)
(yy : D y),
Tl xx (id_disp yy) =
transportb
  (mor_disp (T xx yy)
     (T xx yy))
  (bifunctor_leftid V x y)
  (id_disp (T xx yy))
B_inv: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
B xx yy ;; B yy xx =
transportb (mor_disp (T xx yy) (T xx yy))
  (sym_mon_braiding_inv V x y)
  (id_disp (T xx yy))
x, y: V
xx: D x
yy: D y
! sym_mon_braiding_inv V x y @
cancel_postcomposition ((pr12 V) x y)
  ((pr12 V) x y · identity (y ⊗_{ V} x))
  ((pr12 V) y x) (! id_right ((pr12 V) x y)) @
cancel_postcomposition
  ((pr12 V) x y · identity (y ⊗_{ V} x))
  ((pr12 V) x y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} identity x)
  ((pr12 V) y x)
  (maponpaths (compose ((pr12 V) x y))
     (! bifunctor_leftid V y x)) @
maponpaths_2 compose
  (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x x y
     (identity x)) ((pr12 V) y x) @
assoc' (identity x ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x y)
  ((pr12 V) y x) @
maponpaths (compose (identity x ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
  (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x y)) @
id_right (identity x ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) =
! bifunctor_rightid V y x

    apply homset_property.
  Qed.

  Context (disp_lwhisker_preserves_comp
    : ∏ (x y1 y2 y3 : V) (g1 : V⟦ y1, y2 ⟧) (g2 : V⟦ y2, y3 ⟧) (xx : D x)
        (yy1 : D y1) (yy2 : D y2) (yy3 : D y3)
        (gg1 : yy1 -->[ g1] yy2) (gg2 : yy2 -->[ g2] yy3),
      Tl xx (gg1 ;; gg2)
      = transportb _ (bifunctor_leftcomp V x y1 y2 y3 g1 g2)
          (Tl _ gg1 ;; Tl _ gg2)).

xx2: D x2
xx3: D x3
yy: D y
ff1: xx1 -->[ f1] xx2
ff2: xx2 -->[ f2] xx3
transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx3 yy))
  (maponpaths_2 compose
     (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1 x3 y
        (f1 · f2)) ((pr12 V) y x3) @
   assoc' ((f1 · f2) ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x3 y)
     ((pr12 V) y x3) @
   maponpaths (compose ((f1 · f2) ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
     (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x3 y)) @
   id_right ((f1 · f2) ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
  (B xx1 yy ;; Tl yy (ff1 ;; ff2) ;; B yy xx3) =
transportb (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx3 yy))
  (bifunctor_rightcomp V y x1 x2 x3 f1 f2)
  (transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx2 yy))
     (maponpaths_2 compose
        (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1 x2 y
           f1) ((pr12 V) y x2) @
      assoc' (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x2 y)
        ((pr12 V) y x2) @
      maponpaths (compose (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
        (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x2 y)) @
      id_right (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
     (B xx1 yy ;; Tl yy ff1 ;; B yy xx2) ;; transportf
                                              (mor_disp
                                                 (T
                                                 xx2
                                                 yy)
                                                 (T
                                                 xx3
                                                 yy))
                                              (maponpaths_2
                                                 compose
                                                 (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right
                                                 V x2
                                                 x3 y
                                                 f2)
                                                 ((pr12 V)
                                                 y x3) @
                                               assoc'
                                                 (f2
                                                 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)
                                                 (pr1
                                                 V x3
                                                 y)
                                                 ((pr12 V)
                                                 y x3) @
                                               maponpaths
                                                 (compose
                                                 (f2
                                                 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
                                                 (pr1
                                                 ((pr122 
                                                 (pr2
                                                 V))
                                                 x3 y)) @
                                               id_right
                                                 (f2
                                                 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
                                              (B xx2
                                                 yy ;; 
                                               Tl yy
                                                 ff2 ;; 
                                               B yy
                                                 xx3))

   assoc' (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) 
     (V x2 y) (sym_mon_braiding V y x2) @
   maponpaths (compose (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
     (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x2 y)) @
   id_right (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) t: ∏ (x1 x2 y : V) (f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧) 
(xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2) 
(yy : D y),
xx1 -->[ f] xx2
→ T xx1 yy -->[ f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y] T xx2 yy
disp_lwhisker_preserves_id: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x)
(yy : D y),
Tl xx (id_disp yy) =
transportb
  (mor_disp (T xx yy)
     (T xx yy))
  (bifunctor_leftid V x y)
  (id_disp (T xx yy))
B_inv: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
B xx yy ;; B yy xx =
transportb (mor_disp (T xx yy) (T xx yy))
  (sym_mon_braiding_inv V x y)
  (id_disp (T xx yy))
disp_lwhisker_preserves_comp: ∏ (x y1 y2 y3 : V)
(g1 : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧)
(g2 : V ⟦ y2, y3 ⟧)
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1)
(yy2 : D y2)
(yy3 : D y3)
(gg1 : yy1 -->[ g1] yy2)
(gg2 : yy2 -->[ g2] yy3),
Tl xx (gg1 ;; gg2) =
transportb
  (mor_disp (T xx yy1)
     (T xx yy3))
  (bifunctor_leftcomp V
     x y1 y2 y3 g1 g2)
  (Tl xx gg1 ;; Tl xx
                  gg2)
x1, x2, x3, y: V
f1: V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧
f2: V ⟦ x2, x3 ⟧
xx1: D x1
xx2: D x2
xx3: D x3
yy: D y
ff1: xx1 -->[ f1] xx2
ff2: xx2 -->[ f2] xx3
transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx3 yy))
  (maponpaths_2 compose
     (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1 x3 y
        (f1 · f2)) ((pr12 V) y x3) @
   assoc' ((f1 · f2) ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x3 y)
     ((pr12 V) y x3) @
   maponpaths (compose ((f1 · f2) ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
     (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x3 y)) @
   id_right ((f1 · f2) ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
  (transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T yy xx3))
     (maponpaths (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y))
        (! bifunctor_leftcomp V y x1 x2 x3 f1 f2))
     (B xx1 yy ;; (Tl yy ff1 ;; Tl yy ff2)) ;; B yy
                                                 xx3) =
transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx3 yy))
  (! bifunctor_rightcomp V y x1 x2 x3 f1 f2)
  (transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx3 yy))
     (maponpaths (compose (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
        (maponpaths_2 compose
           (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x2 x3
              y f2) ((pr12 V) y x3) @
         assoc' (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x3 y)
           ((pr12 V) y x3) @
         maponpaths (compose (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
           (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x3 y)) @
         id_right (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)))
     (transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx2 yy))
        (maponpaths_2 compose
           (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1 x2
              y f1) ((pr12 V) y x2) @
         assoc' (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x2 y)
           ((pr12 V) y x2) @
         maponpaths (compose (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
           (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x2 y)) @
         id_right (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
        (B xx1 yy ;; Tl yy ff1 ;; B yy xx2) ;; (B xx2
                                                 yy ;; 
                                                Tl yy
                                                 ff2 ;; 
                                                B yy
                                                 xx3)))

disp_lwhisker_preserves_comp: ∏ (x y1 y2 y3 : V)
(g1 : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧)
(g2 : V ⟦ y2, y3 ⟧)
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1)

  (mor_disp (T xx yy1)

x1, x2, x3, y: V
f1: V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧
f2: V ⟦ x2, x3 ⟧
xx1: D x1
xx2: D x2
xx3: D x3
yy: D y
ff1: xx1 -->[ f1] xx2
ff2: xx2 -->[ f2] xx3
transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx3 yy))
  (maponpaths_2 compose
     (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1 x3 y
        (f1 · f2)) ((pr12 V) y x3) @
   assoc' ((f1 · f2) ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x3 y)
     ((pr12 V) y x3) @
   maponpaths (compose ((f1 · f2) ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
     (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x3 y)) @
   id_right ((f1 · f2) ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
  (transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx3 yy))
     (cancel_postcomposition
        ((pr12 V) x1 y
         · (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1 · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2))
        ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} (f1 · f2))
        ((pr12 V) y x3)
        (maponpaths (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y))
           (! bifunctor_leftcomp V y x1 x2 x3 f1 f2)))
     (B xx1 yy ;; (Tl yy ff1 ;; Tl yy ff2) ;; B yy xx3)) =
transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx3 yy))
  (! bifunctor_rightcomp V y x1 x2 x3 f1 f2)
  (transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx3 yy))
     (maponpaths (compose (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
        (maponpaths_2 compose
           (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x2 x3
              y f2) ((pr12 V) y x3) @
         assoc' (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x3 y)
           ((pr12 V) y x3) @
         maponpaths (compose (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
           (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x3 y)) @
         id_right (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)))
     (transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx3 yy))
        (cancel_postcomposition
           ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1
            · (pr12 V) y x2) (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)
           ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2
            · (pr12 V) y x3)
           (maponpaths_2 compose
              (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1
                 x2 y f1) ((pr12 V) y x2) @
            assoc' (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x2 y)
              ((pr12 V) y x2) @
            maponpaths (compose (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
              (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x2 y)) @
            id_right (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)))
        (B xx1 yy ;; Tl yy ff1 ;; B yy xx2 ;; (B xx2
                                                 yy ;; 
                                               Tl yy
                                                 ff2 ;; 
                                               B yy
                                                 xx3))))

  (cancel_postcomposition
     ((pr12 V) x1 y
      · (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1 · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2))
     ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} (f1 · f2))
     ((pr12 V) y x3)
     (maponpaths (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y))
        (! bifunctor_leftcomp V y x1 x2 x3 f1 f2)) @
   maponpaths_2 compose
     (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1 x3 y

     (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x3 y)) @

  (B xx1 yy ;; (Tl yy ff1 ;; Tl yy ff2) ;; B yy xx3) =

  (cancel_postcomposition
     ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1 · (pr12 V) y x2)
     (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)
     ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2 · (pr12 V) y x3)
     (maponpaths_2 compose
        (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1 x2 y
           f1) ((pr12 V) y x2) @
      assoc' (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x2 y)
        ((pr12 V) y x2) @
      maponpaths (compose (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
        (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x2 y)) @
      id_right (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) @
   maponpaths (compose (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
     (maponpaths_2 compose
        (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x2 x3 y
           f2) ((pr12 V) y x3) @
      assoc' (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x3 y)
        ((pr12 V) y x3) @
      maponpaths (compose (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
        (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x3 y)) @
      id_right (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) @
   ! bifunctor_rightcomp V y x1 x2 x3 f1 f2)

                                         Tl yy ff2 ;; 
                                         B yy xx3))

(yy2 : D y2) (gg : yy1 -->[ g] yy2),
disp_lwhisker x y1 y2 g xx yy1 yy2 gg: ∏ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧) 
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
(yy2 : D y2),
yy1 -->[ g] yy2
→ T xx yy1 -->[ x ⊗^{ V}_{l} g] T xx yy2
disp_braiding: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
T xx yy -->[
sym_mon_braiding V x y] 
T yy xx
B:= λ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y), disp_braiding x y xx yy: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
T xx yy -->[ sym_mon_braiding V x y] T yy xx
Tr:= λ (x1 x2 y : V) (f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧) 
(xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2) 
(yy : D y) (ff : xx1 -->[ f] xx2),
let t := B xx1 yy ;; Tl yy ff ;; B yy xx2 in
transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx2 yy))
  (maponpaths_2 compose
     (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1 x2 y
        f) (sym_mon_braiding V y x2) @
   assoc' (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) 
     (V x2 y) (sym_mon_braiding V y x2) @
   maponpaths (compose (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
     (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x2 y)) @
   id_right (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) t: ∏ (x1 x2 y : V) (f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧) 
(xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2) 
(yy : D y),
xx1 -->[ f] xx2
→ T xx1 yy -->[ f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y] T xx2 yy
disp_lwhisker_preserves_id: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x)
(yy : D y),
Tl xx (id_disp yy) =
transportb
  (mor_disp (T xx yy)
     (T xx yy))
  (bifunctor_leftid V x y)
  (id_disp (T xx yy))
B_inv: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
B xx yy ;; B yy xx =
transportb (mor_disp (T xx yy) (T xx yy))
  (sym_mon_braiding_inv V x y)
  (id_disp (T xx yy))
disp_lwhisker_preserves_comp: ∏ (x y1 y2 y3 : V)
(g1 : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧)
(g2 : V ⟦ y2, y3 ⟧)
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1)
(yy2 : D y2)
(yy3 : D y3)
(gg1 : yy1 -->[ g1] yy2)
(gg2 : yy2 -->[ g2] yy3),
Tl xx (gg1 ;; gg2) =
transportb
  (mor_disp (T xx yy1)
     (T xx yy3))
  (bifunctor_leftcomp V
     x y1 y2 y3 g1 g2)
  (Tl xx gg1 ;; Tl xx
                  gg2)
x1, x2, x3, y: V
f1: V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧
f2: V ⟦ x2, x3 ⟧
xx1: D x1
xx2: D x2
xx3: D x3
yy: D y
ff1: xx1 -->[ f1] xx2
ff2: xx2 -->[ f2] xx3
?b =
transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx3 yy))
  (cancel_postcomposition
     ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1 · (pr12 V) y x2)
     (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)
     ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2 · (pr12 V) y x3)
     (maponpaths_2 compose
        (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1 x2 y
           f1) ((pr12 V) y x2) @
      assoc' (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) 
        (pr1 V x2 y) 
        ((pr12 V) y x2) @
      maponpaths (compose (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
        (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x2 y)) @
      id_right (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) @
   maponpaths (compose (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
     (maponpaths_2 compose
        (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x2 x3 y
           f2) ((pr12 V) y x3) @
      assoc' (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) 
        (pr1 V x3 y) 
        ((pr12 V) y x3) @
      maponpaths (compose (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
        (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x3 y)) @
      id_right (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) @
   ! bifunctor_rightcomp V y x1 x2 x3 f1 f2)
  (B xx1 yy ;; Tl yy ff1 ;; 
   B yy xx2 ;; (B xx2 yy ;; Tl yy ff2 ;; B yy xx3))

yy1 -->[ g] yy2
→ T xx yy1 -->[
  x ⊗^{ V}_{l} g] T xx yy2
Tl:= λ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧) 
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
(yy2 : D y2) (gg : yy1 -->[ g] yy2),
disp_lwhisker x y1 y2 g xx yy1 yy2 gg: ∏ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧) 
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
(yy2 : D y2),
yy1 -->[ g] yy2
→ T xx yy1 -->[ x ⊗^{ V}_{l} g] T xx yy2
disp_braiding: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
T xx yy -->[
sym_mon_braiding V x y] 
T yy xx
B:= λ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y), disp_braiding x y xx yy: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
T xx yy -->[ sym_mon_braiding V x y] T yy xx
Tr:= λ (x1 x2 y : V) (f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧) 
(xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2) 
(yy : D y) (ff : xx1 -->[ f] xx2),
let t := B xx1 yy ;; Tl yy ff ;; B yy xx2 in
transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx2 yy))
  (maponpaths_2 compose
     (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1 x2 y
        f) (sym_mon_braiding V y x2) @
   assoc' (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) 
     (V x2 y) (sym_mon_braiding V y x2) @
   maponpaths (compose (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
     (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x2 y)) @
   id_right (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) t: ∏ (x1 x2 y : V) (f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧) 
(xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2) 
(yy : D y),
xx1 -->[ f] xx2
→ T xx1 yy -->[ f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y] T xx2 yy
disp_lwhisker_preserves_id: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x)
(yy : D y),
Tl xx (id_disp yy) =
transportb
  (mor_disp (T xx yy)
     (T xx yy))
  (bifunctor_leftid V x y)
  (id_disp (T xx yy))
B_inv: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
B xx yy ;; B yy xx =
transportb (mor_disp (T xx yy) (T xx yy))
  (sym_mon_braiding_inv V x y)
  (id_disp (T xx yy))
disp_lwhisker_preserves_comp: ∏ (x y1 y2 y3 : V)
(g1 : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧)
(g2 : V ⟦ y2, y3 ⟧)
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1)
(yy2 : D y2)
(yy3 : D y3)
(gg1 : yy1 -->[ g1] yy2)
(gg2 : yy2 -->[ g2] yy3),
Tl xx (gg1 ;; gg2) =
transportb
  (mor_disp (T xx yy1)
     (T xx yy3))
  (bifunctor_leftcomp V
     x y1 y2 y3 g1 g2)
  (Tl xx gg1 ;; Tl xx
                  gg2)
x1, x2, x3, y: V
f1: V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧
f2: V ⟦ x2, x3 ⟧
xx1: D x1
xx2: D x2
xx3: D x3
yy: D y
ff1: xx1 -->[ f1] xx2
ff2: xx2 -->[ f2] xx3
?t1 =
transportb (mor_disp (T yy xx2) (T xx3 yy))
  (assoc ((pr12 V) y x2)
     ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2) ((pr12 V) y x3))
  (B yy xx2 ;; (B xx2 yy ;; Tl yy ff2) ;; B yy xx3)

  (sym_mon_braiding_inv V x y)
  (id_disp (T xx yy))
disp_lwhisker_preserves_comp: ∏ (x y1 y2 y3 : V)
(g1 : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧)
(g2 : V ⟦ y2, y3 ⟧)

(yy2 : D y2)
(yy3 : D y3)

     (T xx yy3))

ff1: xx1 -->[ f1] xx2
ff2: xx2 -->[ f2] xx3
?y = B yy xx2 ;; B xx2 yy

      apply pathsinv0, B_inv.

D: disp_cat V
disp_tensor_ob: ∏ x y : V, D x → D y → D (x ⊗ y)

(yy : D y), disp_tensor_ob x y xx yy: ∏ x y : V, D x → D y → D (x ⊗ y)
disp_lwhisker: ∏ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧)
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
(yy2 : D y2),
yy1 -->[ g] yy2
→ T xx yy1 -->[
  x ⊗^{ V}_{l} g] T xx yy2
Tl:= λ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧) 
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
(yy2 : D y2) (gg : yy1 -->[ g] yy2),

(yy2 : D y2),
yy1 -->[ g] yy2
→ T xx yy1 -->[ x ⊗^{ V}_{l} g] T xx yy2
disp_braiding: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
T xx yy -->[
sym_mon_braiding V x y] 
T yy xx
B:= λ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y), disp_braiding x y xx yy: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
T xx yy -->[ sym_mon_braiding V x y] T yy xx
Tr:= λ (x1 x2 y : V) (f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧) 
(xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2) 
(yy : D y) (ff : xx1 -->[ f] xx2),
let t := B xx1 yy ;; Tl yy ff ;; B yy xx2 in
transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx2 yy))
  (maponpaths_2 compose
     (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1 x2 y
        f) (sym_mon_braiding V y x2) @
   assoc' (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) 
     (V x2 y) (sym_mon_braiding V y x2) @
   maponpaths (compose (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
     (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x2 y)) @
   id_right (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) t: ∏ (x1 x2 y : V) (f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧) 
(xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2) 
(yy : D y),
xx1 -->[ f] xx2
→ T xx1 yy -->[ f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y] T xx2 yy

(yy : D y),
Tl xx (id_disp yy) =
transportb
  (mor_disp (T xx yy)
     (T xx yy))
  (bifunctor_leftid V x y)
  (id_disp (T xx yy))

(yy : D y),

  (sym_mon_braiding_inv V x y)
  (id_disp (T xx yy))
disp_lwhisker_preserves_comp: ∏ (x y1 y2 y3 : V)
(g1 : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧)
(g2 : V ⟦ y2, y3 ⟧)
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1)
(yy2 : D y2)
(yy3 : D y3)
(gg1 : yy1 -->[ g1] yy2)
(gg2 : yy2 -->[ g2] yy3),
Tl xx (gg1 ;; gg2) =
transportb
  (mor_disp (T xx yy1)
     (T xx yy3))
  (bifunctor_leftcomp V
     x y1 y2 y3 g1 g2)
  (Tl xx gg1 ;; Tl xx
                  gg2)
x1, x2, x3, y: V
f1: V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧
f2: V ⟦ x2, x3 ⟧
xx1: D x1
xx2: D x2
xx3: D x3
yy: D y
ff1: xx1 -->[ f1] xx2
ff2: xx2 -->[ f2] xx3
transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx3 yy))
  (cancel_postcomposition
     ((pr12 V) x1 y
      · (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1 · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2))
     ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} (f1 · f2))
     ((pr12 V) y x3)
     (maponpaths (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y))
        (! bifunctor_leftcomp V y x1 x2 x3 f1 f2)) @
   maponpaths_2 compose
     (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1 x3 y
        (f1 · f2)) ((pr12 V) y x3) @
   assoc' ((f1 · f2) ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x3 y)
     ((pr12 V) y x3) @
   maponpaths (compose ((f1 · f2) ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
     (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x3 y)) @
   id_right ((f1 · f2) ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
  (B xx1 yy ;; (Tl yy ff1 ;; Tl yy ff2) ;; B yy xx3) =
transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx3 yy))
  (cancel_postcomposition
     ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1 · (pr12 V) y x2)
     (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)
     ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2 · (pr12 V) y x3)
     (maponpaths_2 compose
        (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1 x2 y
           f1) ((pr12 V) y x2) @
      assoc' (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x2 y)
        ((pr12 V) y x2) @
      maponpaths (compose (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
        (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x2 y)) @
      id_right (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) @
   maponpaths (compose (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
     (maponpaths_2 compose
        (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x2 x3 y
           f2) ((pr12 V) y x3) @
      assoc' (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x3 y)
        ((pr12 V) y x3) @
      maponpaths (compose (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
        (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x3 y)) @
      id_right (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) @
   ! bifunctor_rightcomp V y x1 x2 x3 f1 f2)
  (transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx3 yy))
     (assoc ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1)
        ((pr12 V) y x2)
        ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2
         · (pr12 V) y x3))
     (B xx1 yy ;; Tl yy ff1 ;; transportb
                                 (mor_disp (T yy xx2)
                                    (T xx3 yy))
                                 (assoc
                                    ((pr12 V) y x2)
                                    ((pr12 V) x2 y
                                     · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
                                    ((pr12 V) y x3))
                                 (transportb
                                    (mor_disp
                                       (T yy xx2)
                                       (T yy xx3))
                                    (assoc
                                       ((pr12 V) y x2)
                                       ((pr12 V) x2 y)
                                       (y
                                        ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2))
                                    (transportb
                                       (mor_disp
                                          (T yy xx2)
                                          (T yy xx2))
                                       (sym_mon_braiding_inv
                                          V y x2)
                                       (id_disp
                                          (T yy xx2)) ;; 
                                     Tl yy ff2) ;; 
                                  B yy xx3)))

                                    (id_disp
                                       (T yy xx2)) ;; 
                                  Tl yy ff2) ;; B yy
                                                 xx3))

    
V: sym_monoidal_cat
D: disp_cat V
disp_tensor_ob: ∏ x y : V, D x → D y → D (x ⊗ y)
T:= λ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y), disp_tensor_ob x y xx yy: ∏ x y : V, D x → D y → D (x ⊗ y)
disp_lwhisker: ∏ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧)
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
(yy2 : D y2),
yy1 -->[ g] yy2
→ T xx yy1 -->[
  x ⊗^{ V}_{l} g] T xx yy2
Tl:= λ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧) 
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
(yy2 : D y2) (gg : yy1 -->[ g] yy2),
disp_lwhisker x y1 y2 g xx yy1 yy2 gg: ∏ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧) 
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
(yy2 : D y2),
yy1 -->[ g] yy2
→ T xx yy1 -->[ x ⊗^{ V}_{l} g] T xx yy2
disp_braiding: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
T xx yy -->[
sym_mon_braiding V x y] 
T yy xx
B:= λ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y), disp_braiding x y xx yy: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
T xx yy -->[ sym_mon_braiding V x y] T yy xx
Tr:= λ (x1 x2 y : V) (f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧) 
(xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2) 
(yy : D y) (ff : xx1 -->[ f] xx2),
let t := B xx1 yy ;; Tl yy ff ;; B yy xx2 in
transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx2 yy))
  (maponpaths_2 compose
     (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1 x2 y
        f) (sym_mon_braiding V y x2) @
   assoc' (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) 
     (V x2 y) (sym_mon_braiding V y x2) @
   maponpaths (compose (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
     (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x2 y)) @
   id_right (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) t: ∏ (x1 x2 y : V) (f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧) 
(xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2) 
(yy : D y),
xx1 -->[ f] xx2
→ T xx1 yy -->[ f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y] T xx2 yy
disp_lwhisker_preserves_id: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x)
(yy : D y),
Tl xx (id_disp yy) =
transportb
  (mor_disp (T xx yy)
     (T xx yy))
  (bifunctor_leftid V x y)
  (id_disp (T xx yy))
B_inv: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
B xx yy ;; B yy xx =
transportb (mor_disp (T xx yy) (T xx yy))
  (sym_mon_braiding_inv V x y)
  (id_disp (T xx yy))
disp_lwhisker_preserves_comp: ∏ (x y1 y2 y3 : V)
(g1 : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧)
(g2 : V ⟦ y2, y3 ⟧)
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1)
(yy2 : D y2)
(yy3 : D y3)
(gg1 : yy1 -->[ g1] yy2)
(gg2 : yy2 -->[ g2] yy3),
Tl xx (gg1 ;; gg2) =
transportb
  (mor_disp (T xx yy1)
     (T xx yy3))
  (bifunctor_leftcomp V
     x y1 y2 y3 g1 g2)
  (Tl xx gg1 ;; Tl xx
                  gg2)
x1, x2, x3, y: V
f1: V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧
f2: V ⟦ x2, x3 ⟧
xx1: D x1
xx2: D x2
xx3: D x3
yy: D y
ff1: xx1 -->[ f1] xx2
ff2: xx2 -->[ f2] xx3
transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx3 yy))
  (cancel_postcomposition
     ((pr12 V) x1 y
      · (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1 · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2))
     ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} (f1 · f2))
     ((pr12 V) y x3)
     (maponpaths (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y))
        (! bifunctor_leftcomp V y x1 x2 x3 f1 f2)) @
   maponpaths_2 compose
     (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1 x3 y
        (f1 · f2)) ((pr12 V) y x3) @
   assoc' ((f1 · f2) ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x3 y)
     ((pr12 V) y x3) @
   maponpaths (compose ((f1 · f2) ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
     (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x3 y)) @
   id_right ((f1 · f2) ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
  (B xx1 yy ;; (Tl yy ff1 ;; Tl yy ff2) ;; B yy xx3) =
transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx3 yy))
  (assoc ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1)
     ((pr12 V) y x2)
     ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2 · (pr12 V) y x3) @
   cancel_postcomposition
     ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1 · (pr12 V) y x2)
     (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)
     ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2 · (pr12 V) y x3)
     (maponpaths_2 compose
        (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1 x2 y
           f1) ((pr12 V) y x2) @
      assoc' (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x2 y)
        ((pr12 V) y x2) @
      maponpaths (compose (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
        (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x2 y)) @
      id_right (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) @
   maponpaths (compose (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
     (maponpaths_2 compose
        (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x2 x3 y
           f2) ((pr12 V) y x3) @
      assoc' (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x3 y)
        ((pr12 V) y x3) @
      maponpaths (compose (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
        (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x3 y)) @
      id_right (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) @
   ! bifunctor_rightcomp V y x1 x2 x3 f1 f2)
  (transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx3 yy))
     (maponpaths
        (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1))
        (! assoc ((pr12 V) y x2)
             ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
             ((pr12 V) y x3)))
     (B xx1 yy ;; Tl yy ff1 ;; (transportf
                                  (mor_disp (T yy xx2)
                                     (T yy xx3))
                                  (! assoc
                                       ((pr12 V) y x2)
                                       ((pr12 V) x2 y)
                                       (y
                                        ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2))
                                  (transportf
                                     (mor_disp
                                        (T yy xx2)
                                        (T yy xx2))
                                     (! sym_mon_braiding_inv
                                          V y x2)
                                     (id_disp
                                        (T yy xx2)) ;; 
                                   Tl yy ff2) ;; B yy
                                                 xx3)))

(yy : D y),

sym_mon_braiding V x y] 
T yy xx
B:= λ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y), disp_braiding x y xx yy: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
T xx yy -->[ sym_mon_braiding V x y] T yy xx
Tr:= λ (x1 x2 y : V) (f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧) 
(xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2) 
(yy : D y) (ff : xx1 -->[ f] xx2),
let t := B xx1 yy ;; Tl yy ff ;; B yy xx2 in
transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx2 yy))
  (maponpaths_2 compose
     (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1 x2 y
        f) (sym_mon_braiding V y x2) @
   assoc' (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) 
     (V x2 y) (sym_mon_braiding V y x2) @
   maponpaths (compose (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
     (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x2 y)) @
   id_right (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) t: ∏ (x1 x2 y : V) (f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧) 
(xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2) 
(yy : D y),
xx1 -->[ f] xx2
→ T xx1 yy -->[ f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y] T xx2 yy
disp_lwhisker_preserves_id: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x)
(yy : D y),
Tl xx (id_disp yy) =
transportb
  (mor_disp (T xx yy)
     (T xx yy))
  (bifunctor_leftid V x y)
  (id_disp (T xx yy))
B_inv: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
B xx yy ;; B yy xx =
transportb (mor_disp (T xx yy) (T xx yy))
  (sym_mon_braiding_inv V x y)
  (id_disp (T xx yy))
disp_lwhisker_preserves_comp: ∏ (x y1 y2 y3 : V)
(g1 : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧)
(g2 : V ⟦ y2, y3 ⟧)
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1)
(yy2 : D y2)
(yy3 : D y3)
(gg1 : yy1 -->[ g1] yy2)
(gg2 : yy2 -->[ g2] yy3),
Tl xx (gg1 ;; gg2) =
transportb
  (mor_disp (T xx yy1)
     (T xx yy3))
  (bifunctor_leftcomp V
     x y1 y2 y3 g1 g2)
  (Tl xx gg1 ;; Tl xx
                  gg2)
x1, x2, x3, y: V
f1: V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧
f2: V ⟦ x2, x3 ⟧
xx1: D x1
xx2: D x2
xx3: D x3
yy: D y
ff1: xx1 -->[ f1] xx2
ff2: xx2 -->[ f2] xx3
transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx3 yy))
  (cancel_postcomposition
     ((pr12 V) x1 y
      · (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1 · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2))
     ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} (f1 · f2))
     ((pr12 V) y x3)
     (maponpaths (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y))
        (! bifunctor_leftcomp V y x1 x2 x3 f1 f2)) @
   maponpaths_2 compose
     (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1 x3 y
        (f1 · f2)) ((pr12 V) y x3) @
   assoc' ((f1 · f2) ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x3 y)
     ((pr12 V) y x3) @
   maponpaths (compose ((f1 · f2) ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
     (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x3 y)) @
   id_right ((f1 · f2) ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
  (B xx1 yy ;; (Tl yy ff1 ;; Tl yy ff2) ;; B yy xx3) =
transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx3 yy))
  (maponpaths
     (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1))
     (! assoc ((pr12 V) y x2)
          ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
          ((pr12 V) y x3)) @
   assoc ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1)
     ((pr12 V) y x2)
     ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2 · (pr12 V) y x3) @
   cancel_postcomposition
     ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1 · (pr12 V) y x2)
     (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)
     ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2 · (pr12 V) y x3)
     (maponpaths_2 compose
        (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1 x2 y
           f1) ((pr12 V) y x2) @
      assoc' (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x2 y)
        ((pr12 V) y x2) @
      maponpaths (compose (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
        (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x2 y)) @
      id_right (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) @
   maponpaths (compose (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
     (maponpaths_2 compose
        (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x2 x3 y
           f2) ((pr12 V) y x3) @
      assoc' (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x3 y)
        ((pr12 V) y x3) @
      maponpaths (compose (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
        (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x3 y)) @
      id_right (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) @
   ! bifunctor_rightcomp V y x1 x2 x3 f1 f2)
  (B xx1 yy ;; Tl yy ff1 ;; transportf
                              (mor_disp (T yy xx2)
                                 (T xx3 yy))
                              (cancel_postcomposition
                                 ((pr12 V) y x2
                                  · (pr12 V) x2 y
                                  · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
                                 ((pr12 V) y x2
                                  · ((pr12 V) x2 y
                                     · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2))
                                 ((pr12 V) y x3)
                                 (! assoc
                                      ((pr12 V) y x2)
                                      ((pr12 V) x2 y)
                                      (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)))
                              (transportf
                                 (mor_disp (T yy xx2)
                                    (T xx3 yy))
                                 (cancel_postcomposition
                                    (identity (y ⊗ x2)
                                     · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
                                    ((pr12 V) y x2
                                     · (pr12 V) x2 y
                                     · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
                                    ((pr12 V) y x3)
                                    (cancel_postcomposition
                                       (identity
                                          (y ⊗ x2))
                                       ((pr12 V) y x2
                                        · (pr12 V) x2
                                            y)
                                       (y
                                        ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
                                       (! sym_mon_braiding_inv
                                            V y x2)))
                                 (id_disp (T yy xx2) ;; 
                                  Tl yy ff2 ;; B yy
                                                 xx3)))

        (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1 x2 y
           f1) ((pr12 V) y x2) @
      assoc' (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x2 y)
        ((pr12 V) y x2) @
      maponpaths (compose (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
        (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x2 y)) @
      id_right (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) @
   maponpaths (compose (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
     (maponpaths_2 compose
        (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x2 x3 y
           f2) ((pr12 V) y x3) @
      assoc' (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x3 y)

     (maponpaths
        (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1))

           ((pr12 V) y x2 · (pr12 V) x2 y

     ((pr12 V) y x3)

   maponpaths (compose ((f1 · f2) ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
     (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x3 y)) @

  (B xx1 yy ;; (Tl yy ff1 ;; Tl yy ff2) ;; B yy xx3) =

  (maponpaths
     (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1))
     (cancel_postcomposition
        (identity (y ⊗ x2) · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
        ((pr12 V) y x2 · (pr12 V) x2 y

           ((pr12 V) y x2 · (pr12 V) x2 y)
           (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
           (! sym_mon_braiding_inv V y x2))) @
   maponpaths
     (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1))
     (cancel_postcomposition
        ((pr12 V) y x2 · (pr12 V) x2 y
         · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
        ((pr12 V) y x2
         · ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2))
        ((pr12 V) y x3)
        (! assoc ((pr12 V) y x2) ((pr12 V) x2 y)
             (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2))) @
   maponpaths
     (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1))
     (! assoc ((pr12 V) y x2)
          ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
          ((pr12 V) y x3)) @
   assoc ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1)
     ((pr12 V) y x2)
     ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2 · (pr12 V) y x3) @
   cancel_postcomposition
     ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1 · (pr12 V) y x2)
     (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)
     ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2 · (pr12 V) y x3)
     (maponpaths_2 compose
        (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1 x2 y
           f1) ((pr12 V) y x2) @
      assoc' (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x2 y)
        ((pr12 V) y x2) @
      maponpaths (compose (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
        (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x2 y)) @
      id_right (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) @
   maponpaths (compose (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
     (maponpaths_2 compose
        (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x2 x3 y
           f2) ((pr12 V) y x3) @
      assoc' (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x3 y)
        ((pr12 V) y x3) @
      maponpaths (compose (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
        (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x3 y)) @
      id_right (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) @
   ! bifunctor_rightcomp V y x1 x2 x3 f1 f2)
  (B xx1 yy ;; Tl yy ff1 ;; (id_disp (T yy xx2) ;; 
                             Tl yy ff2 ;; B yy xx3))

    
V: sym_monoidal_cat
D: disp_cat V
disp_tensor_ob: ∏ x y : V, D x → D y → D (x ⊗ y)

(yy : D y), disp_tensor_ob x y xx yy: ∏ x y : V, D x → D y → D (x ⊗ y)
disp_lwhisker: ∏ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧)
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
(yy2 : D y2),
yy1 -->[ g] yy2
→ T xx yy1 -->[
  x ⊗^{ V}_{l} g] T xx yy2
Tl:= λ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧) 
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
(yy2 : D y2) (gg : yy1 -->[ g] yy2),
disp_lwhisker x y1 y2 g xx yy1 yy2 gg: ∏ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧) 
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
(yy2 : D y2),
yy1 -->[ g] yy2
→ T xx yy1 -->[ x ⊗^{ V}_{l} g] T xx yy2
disp_braiding: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
T xx yy -->[
sym_mon_braiding V x y] 
T yy xx
B:= λ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y), disp_braiding x y xx yy: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
T xx yy -->[ sym_mon_braiding V x y] T yy xx
Tr:= λ (x1 x2 y : V) (f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧) 
(xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2) 
(yy : D y) (ff : xx1 -->[ f] xx2),
let t := B xx1 yy ;; Tl yy ff ;; B yy xx2 in
transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx2 yy))
  (maponpaths_2 compose
     (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1 x2 y
        f) (sym_mon_braiding V y x2) @
   assoc' (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) 
     (V x2 y) (sym_mon_braiding V y x2) @
   maponpaths (compose (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
     (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x2 y)) @
   id_right (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) t: ∏ (x1 x2 y : V) (f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧) 
(xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2) 
(yy : D y),
xx1 -->[ f] xx2
→ T xx1 yy -->[ f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y] T xx2 yy
disp_lwhisker_preserves_id: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x)
(yy : D y),
Tl xx (id_disp yy) =
transportb
  (mor_disp (T xx yy)
     (T xx yy))
  (bifunctor_leftid V x y)
  (id_disp (T xx yy))
B_inv: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
B xx yy ;; B yy xx =
transportb (mor_disp (T xx yy) (T xx yy))
  (sym_mon_braiding_inv V x y)
  (id_disp (T xx yy))
disp_lwhisker_preserves_comp: ∏ (x y1 y2 y3 : V)
(g1 : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧)
(g2 : V ⟦ y2, y3 ⟧)
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1)
(yy2 : D y2)
(yy3 : D y3)
(gg1 : yy1 -->[ g1] yy2)
(gg2 : yy2 -->[ g2] yy3),
Tl xx (gg1 ;; gg2) =
transportb
  (mor_disp (T xx yy1)
     (T xx yy3))
  (bifunctor_leftcomp V
     x y1 y2 y3 g1 g2)
  (Tl xx gg1 ;; Tl xx
                  gg2)
x1, x2, x3, y: V
f1: V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧
f2: V ⟦ x2, x3 ⟧
xx1: D x1
xx2: D x2
xx3: D x3
yy: D y
ff1: xx1 -->[ f1] xx2
ff2: xx2 -->[ f2] xx3
transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx3 yy))
  (cancel_postcomposition
     ((pr12 V) x1 y
      · (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1 · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2))
     ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} (f1 · f2))
     ((pr12 V) y x3)
     (maponpaths (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y))
        (! bifunctor_leftcomp V y x1 x2 x3 f1 f2)) @
   maponpaths_2 compose
     (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1 x3 y
        (f1 · f2)) ((pr12 V) y x3) @
   assoc' ((f1 · f2) ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x3 y)
     ((pr12 V) y x3) @
   maponpaths (compose ((f1 · f2) ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
     (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x3 y)) @
   id_right ((f1 · f2) ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
  (B xx1 yy ;; (Tl yy ff1 ;; Tl yy ff2) ;; B yy xx3) =
transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx3 yy))
  (maponpaths
     (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1))
     (cancel_postcomposition
        (identity (y ⊗ x2) · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
        ((pr12 V) y x2 · (pr12 V) x2 y
         · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2) ((pr12 V) y x3)
        (cancel_postcomposition (identity (y ⊗ x2))
           ((pr12 V) y x2 · (pr12 V) x2 y)
           (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
           (! sym_mon_braiding_inv V y x2))) @
   maponpaths
     (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1))
     (cancel_postcomposition
        ((pr12 V) y x2 · (pr12 V) x2 y
         · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
        ((pr12 V) y x2
         · ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2))
        ((pr12 V) y x3)
        (! assoc ((pr12 V) y x2) ((pr12 V) x2 y)
             (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2))) @
   maponpaths
     (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1))
     (! assoc ((pr12 V) y x2)
          ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
          ((pr12 V) y x3)) @
   assoc ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1)
     ((pr12 V) y x2)
     ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2 · (pr12 V) y x3) @
   cancel_postcomposition
     ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1 · (pr12 V) y x2)
     (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)
     ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2 · (pr12 V) y x3)
     (maponpaths_2 compose
        (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1 x2 y
           f1) ((pr12 V) y x2) @
      assoc' (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x2 y)
        ((pr12 V) y x2) @
      maponpaths (compose (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
        (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x2 y)) @
      id_right (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) @
   maponpaths (compose (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
     (maponpaths_2 compose
        (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x2 x3 y
           f2) ((pr12 V) y x3) @
      assoc' (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x3 y)
        ((pr12 V) y x3) @
      maponpaths (compose (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
        (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x3 y)) @
      id_right (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) @
   ! bifunctor_rightcomp V y x1 x2 x3 f1 f2)
  (B xx1 yy ;; Tl yy ff1 ;; (transportb
                               (mor_disp (T yy xx2)
                                  (T yy xx3))
                               (id_left
                                  (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2))
                               (Tl yy ff2) ;; B yy xx3))

                                 (T xx3 yy))
                              (cancel_postcomposition
                                 (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
                                 (identity (y ⊗ x2)
                                  · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
                                 ((pr12 V) y x3)
                                 (! id_left
                                      (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)))
                              (Tl yy ff2 ;; B yy xx3))

    
V: sym_monoidal_cat
D: disp_cat V
disp_tensor_ob: ∏ x y : V, D x → D y → D (x ⊗ y)
T:= λ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y), disp_tensor_ob x y xx yy: ∏ x y : V, D x → D y → D (x ⊗ y)
disp_lwhisker: ∏ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧)
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
(yy2 : D y2),
yy1 -->[ g] yy2
→ T xx yy1 -->[
  x ⊗^{ V}_{l} g] T xx yy2
Tl:= λ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧) 
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
(yy2 : D y2) (gg : yy1 -->[ g] yy2),
disp_lwhisker x y1 y2 g xx yy1 yy2 gg: ∏ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧) 
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
(yy2 : D y2),
yy1 -->[ g] yy2
→ T xx yy1 -->[ x ⊗^{ V}_{l} g] T xx yy2
disp_braiding: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
T xx yy -->[
sym_mon_braiding V x y] 
T yy xx
B:= λ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y), disp_braiding x y xx yy: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
T xx yy -->[ sym_mon_braiding V x y] T yy xx
Tr:= λ (x1 x2 y : V) (f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧) 
(xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2) 
(yy : D y) (ff : xx1 -->[ f] xx2),
let t := B xx1 yy ;; Tl yy ff ;; B yy xx2 in
transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx2 yy))
  (maponpaths_2 compose
     (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1 x2 y
        f) (sym_mon_braiding V y x2) @
   assoc' (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) 
     (V x2 y) (sym_mon_braiding V y x2) @
   maponpaths (compose (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
     (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x2 y)) @
   id_right (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) t: ∏ (x1 x2 y : V) (f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧) 
(xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2) 
(yy : D y),
xx1 -->[ f] xx2
→ T xx1 yy -->[ f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y] T xx2 yy
disp_lwhisker_preserves_id: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x)
(yy : D y),
Tl xx (id_disp yy) =
transportb
  (mor_disp (T xx yy)
     (T xx yy))
  (bifunctor_leftid V x y)
  (id_disp (T xx yy))
B_inv: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
B xx yy ;; B yy xx =
transportb (mor_disp (T xx yy) (T xx yy))
  (sym_mon_braiding_inv V x y)
  (id_disp (T xx yy))
disp_lwhisker_preserves_comp: ∏ (x y1 y2 y3 : V)
(g1 : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧)
(g2 : V ⟦ y2, y3 ⟧)
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1)
(yy2 : D y2)
(yy3 : D y3)
(gg1 : yy1 -->[ g1] yy2)
(gg2 : yy2 -->[ g2] yy3),
Tl xx (gg1 ;; gg2) =
transportb
  (mor_disp (T xx yy1)
     (T xx yy3))
  (bifunctor_leftcomp V
     x y1 y2 y3 g1 g2)
  (Tl xx gg1 ;; Tl xx
                  gg2)
x1, x2, x3, y: V
f1: V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧
f2: V ⟦ x2, x3 ⟧
xx1: D x1
xx2: D x2
xx3: D x3
yy: D y
ff1: xx1 -->[ f1] xx2
ff2: xx2 -->[ f2] xx3
transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx3 yy))
  (cancel_postcomposition
     ((pr12 V) x1 y
      · (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1 · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2))
     ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} (f1 · f2))
     ((pr12 V) y x3)
     (maponpaths (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y))
        (! bifunctor_leftcomp V y x1 x2 x3 f1 f2)) @
   maponpaths_2 compose
     (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1 x3 y
        (f1 · f2)) ((pr12 V) y x3) @
   assoc' ((f1 · f2) ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x3 y)
     ((pr12 V) y x3) @
   maponpaths (compose ((f1 · f2) ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
     (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x3 y)) @
   id_right ((f1 · f2) ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
  (B xx1 yy ;; (Tl yy ff1 ;; Tl yy ff2) ;; B yy xx3) =
transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx3 yy))
  (maponpaths
     (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1))
     (cancel_postcomposition
        (identity (y ⊗ x2) · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
        ((pr12 V) y x2 · (pr12 V) x2 y
         · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2) ((pr12 V) y x3)
        (cancel_postcomposition (identity (y ⊗ x2))
           ((pr12 V) y x2 · (pr12 V) x2 y)
           (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
           (! sym_mon_braiding_inv V y x2))) @
   maponpaths
     (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1))
     (cancel_postcomposition
        ((pr12 V) y x2 · (pr12 V) x2 y
         · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
        ((pr12 V) y x2
         · ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2))
        ((pr12 V) y x3)
        (! assoc ((pr12 V) y x2) ((pr12 V) x2 y)
             (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2))) @
   maponpaths
     (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1))
     (! assoc ((pr12 V) y x2)
          ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
          ((pr12 V) y x3)) @
   assoc ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1)
     ((pr12 V) y x2)
     ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2 · (pr12 V) y x3) @
   cancel_postcomposition
     ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1 · (pr12 V) y x2)
     (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)
     ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2 · (pr12 V) y x3)
     (maponpaths_2 compose
        (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1 x2 y
           f1) ((pr12 V) y x2) @
      assoc' (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x2 y)
        ((pr12 V) y x2) @
      maponpaths (compose (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
        (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x2 y)) @
      id_right (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) @
   maponpaths (compose (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
     (maponpaths_2 compose
        (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x2 x3 y
           f2) ((pr12 V) y x3) @
      assoc' (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x3 y)
        ((pr12 V) y x3) @
      maponpaths (compose (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
        (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x3 y)) @
      id_right (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) @
   ! bifunctor_rightcomp V y x1 x2 x3 f1 f2)
  (transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx3 yy))
     (maponpaths
        (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1))
        (cancel_postcomposition (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
           (identity (y ⊗ x2) · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
           ((pr12 V) y x3)
           (! id_left (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2))))
     (B xx1 yy ;; Tl yy ff1 ;; (Tl yy ff2 ;; B yy xx3)))

     (maponpaths_2 compose
        (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x2 x3 y
           f2) ((pr12 V) y x3) @
      assoc' (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x3 y)
        ((pr12 V) y x3) @
      maponpaths (compose (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
        (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x3 y)) @
      id_right (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) @
   ! bifunctor_rightcomp V y x1 x2 x3 f1 f2)
  (transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx3 yy))
     (cancel_postcomposition
        ((pr12 V) x1 y
         · (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1 · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2))
        ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} (f1 · f2))
        ((pr12 V) y x3)
        (maponpaths (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y))
           (! bifunctor_leftcomp V y x1 x2 x3 f1 f2)) @
      maponpaths_2 compose
        (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1 x3 y
           (f1 · f2)) ((pr12 V) y x3) @
      assoc' ((f1 · f2) ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x3 y)
        ((pr12 V) y x3) @
      maponpaths (compose ((f1 · f2) ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
        (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x3 y)) @
      id_right ((f1 · f2) ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
     (B xx1 yy ;; (Tl yy ff1 ;; Tl yy ff2) ;; B yy xx3)) =
B xx1 yy ;; Tl yy ff1 ;; (Tl yy ff2 ;; B yy xx3)

    
V: sym_monoidal_cat
D: disp_cat V
disp_tensor_ob: ∏ x y : V, D x → D y → D (x ⊗ y)
T:= λ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y), disp_tensor_ob x y xx yy: ∏ x y : V, D x → D y → D (x ⊗ y)
disp_lwhisker: ∏ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧)
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
(yy2 : D y2),
yy1 -->[ g] yy2
→ T xx yy1 -->[
  x ⊗^{ V}_{l} g] T xx yy2
Tl:= λ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧) 
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
(yy2 : D y2) (gg : yy1 -->[ g] yy2),
disp_lwhisker x y1 y2 g xx yy1 yy2 gg: ∏ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧) 
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
(yy2 : D y2),
yy1 -->[ g] yy2
→ T xx yy1 -->[ x ⊗^{ V}_{l} g] T xx yy2
disp_braiding: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
T xx yy -->[
sym_mon_braiding V x y] 
T yy xx
B:= λ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y), disp_braiding x y xx yy: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
T xx yy -->[ sym_mon_braiding V x y] T yy xx
Tr:= λ (x1 x2 y : V) (f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧) 
(xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2) 
(yy : D y) (ff : xx1 -->[ f] xx2),
let t := B xx1 yy ;; Tl yy ff ;; B yy xx2 in
transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx2 yy))
  (maponpaths_2 compose
     (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1 x2 y
        f) (sym_mon_braiding V y x2) @
   assoc' (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) 
     (V x2 y) (sym_mon_braiding V y x2) @
   maponpaths (compose (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
     (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x2 y)) @
   id_right (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) t: ∏ (x1 x2 y : V) (f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧) 
(xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2) 
(yy : D y),
xx1 -->[ f] xx2
→ T xx1 yy -->[ f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y] T xx2 yy
disp_lwhisker_preserves_id: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x)
(yy : D y),
Tl xx (id_disp yy) =
transportb
  (mor_disp (T xx yy)
     (T xx yy))
  (bifunctor_leftid V x y)
  (id_disp (T xx yy))
B_inv: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
B xx yy ;; B yy xx =
transportb (mor_disp (T xx yy) (T xx yy))
  (sym_mon_braiding_inv V x y)
  (id_disp (T xx yy))
disp_lwhisker_preserves_comp: ∏ (x y1 y2 y3 : V)
(g1 : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧)
(g2 : V ⟦ y2, y3 ⟧)
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1)
(yy2 : D y2)
(yy3 : D y3)
(gg1 : yy1 -->[ g1] yy2)
(gg2 : yy2 -->[ g2] yy3),
Tl xx (gg1 ;; gg2) =
transportb
  (mor_disp (T xx yy1)
     (T xx yy3))
  (bifunctor_leftcomp V
     x y1 y2 y3 g1 g2)
  (Tl xx gg1 ;; Tl xx
                  gg2)
x1, x2, x3, y: V
f1: V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧
f2: V ⟦ x2, x3 ⟧
xx1: D x1
xx2: D x2
xx3: D x3
yy: D y
ff1: xx1 -->[ f1] xx2
ff2: xx2 -->[ f2] xx3
transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx3 yy))
  (! (maponpaths
        (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1))
        (cancel_postcomposition (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
           (identity (y ⊗ x2) · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
           ((pr12 V) y x3)
           (! id_left (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2))) @
      maponpaths
        (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1))
        (cancel_postcomposition
           (identity (y ⊗ x2) · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
           ((pr12 V) y x2 · (pr12 V) x2 y
            · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2) ((pr12 V) y x3)
           (cancel_postcomposition (identity (y ⊗ x2))
              ((pr12 V) y x2 · (pr12 V) x2 y)
              (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
              (! sym_mon_braiding_inv V y x2))) @
      maponpaths
        (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1))
        (cancel_postcomposition
           ((pr12 V) y x2 · (pr12 V) x2 y
            · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
           ((pr12 V) y x2
            · ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2))
           ((pr12 V) y x3)
           (! assoc ((pr12 V) y x2) ((pr12 V) x2 y)
                (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2))) @
      maponpaths
        (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1))
        (! assoc ((pr12 V) y x2)
             ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
             ((pr12 V) y x3)) @
      assoc ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1)
        ((pr12 V) y x2)
        ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2
         · (pr12 V) y x3) @
      cancel_postcomposition
        ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1
         · (pr12 V) y x2) (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)
        ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2
         · (pr12 V) y x3)
        (maponpaths_2 compose
           (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1 x2
              y f1) ((pr12 V) y x2) @
         assoc' (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x2 y)
           ((pr12 V) y x2) @
         maponpaths (compose (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
           (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x2 y)) @
         id_right (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) @
      maponpaths (compose (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
        (maponpaths_2 compose
           (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x2 x3
              y f2) ((pr12 V) y x3) @
         assoc' (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x3 y)
           ((pr12 V) y x3) @
         maponpaths (compose (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
           (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x3 y)) @
         id_right (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) @
      ! bifunctor_rightcomp V y x1 x2 x3 f1 f2))
  (transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx3 yy))
     (cancel_postcomposition
        ((pr12 V) x1 y
         · (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1 · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2))
        ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} (f1 · f2))
        ((pr12 V) y x3)
        (maponpaths (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y))
           (! bifunctor_leftcomp V y x1 x2 x3 f1 f2)) @
      maponpaths_2 compose
        (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1 x3 y
           (f1 · f2)) ((pr12 V) y x3) @
      assoc' ((f1 · f2) ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x3 y)
        ((pr12 V) y x3) @
      maponpaths (compose ((f1 · f2) ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
        (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x3 y)) @
      id_right ((f1 · f2) ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
     (B xx1 yy ;; (Tl yy ff1 ;; Tl yy ff2) ;; B yy xx3)) =
B xx1 yy ;; Tl yy ff1 ;; (Tl yy ff2 ;; B yy xx3)

disp_lwhisker_preserves_comp: ∏ (x y1 y2 y3 : V)

(g2 : V ⟦ y2, y3 ⟧)
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1)

x1, x2, x3, y: V
f1: V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧
f2: V ⟦ x2, x3 ⟧
xx1: D x1
xx2: D x2
xx3: D x3
yy: D y
ff1: xx1 -->[ f1] xx2
ff2: xx2 -->[ f2] xx3

  ((cancel_postcomposition
      ((pr12 V) x1 y
       · (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1 · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2))
      ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} (f1 · f2))
      ((pr12 V) y x3)
      (maponpaths (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y))
         (! bifunctor_leftcomp V y x1 x2 x3 f1 f2)) @
    maponpaths_2 compose
      (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1 x3 y
         (f1 · f2)) ((pr12 V) y x3) @
    assoc' ((f1 · f2) ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x3 y)
      ((pr12 V) y x3) @
    maponpaths (compose ((f1 · f2) ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
      (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x3 y)) @
    id_right ((f1 · f2) ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) @
   ! (maponpaths
        (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1))
        (cancel_postcomposition (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
           (identity (y ⊗ x2) · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
           ((pr12 V) y x3)
           (! id_left (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2))) @
      maponpaths
        (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1))
        (cancel_postcomposition
           (identity (y ⊗ x2) · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
           ((pr12 V) y x2 · (pr12 V) x2 y
            · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2) ((pr12 V) y x3)
           (cancel_postcomposition (identity (y ⊗ x2))
              ((pr12 V) y x2 · (pr12 V) x2 y)
              (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
              (! sym_mon_braiding_inv V y x2))) @
      maponpaths
        (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1))
        (cancel_postcomposition
           ((pr12 V) y x2 · (pr12 V) x2 y
            · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
           ((pr12 V) y x2
            · ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2))
           ((pr12 V) y x3)
           (! assoc ((pr12 V) y x2) ((pr12 V) x2 y)
                (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2))) @
      maponpaths
        (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1))
        (! assoc ((pr12 V) y x2)
             ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
             ((pr12 V) y x3)) @
      assoc ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1)
        ((pr12 V) y x2)
        ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2
         · (pr12 V) y x3) @
      cancel_postcomposition
        ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1
         · (pr12 V) y x2) (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)
        ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2
         · (pr12 V) y x3)
        (maponpaths_2 compose
           (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1 x2
              y f1) ((pr12 V) y x2) @
         assoc' (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x2 y)
           ((pr12 V) y x2) @
         maponpaths (compose (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
           (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x2 y)) @
         id_right (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) @
      maponpaths (compose (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
        (maponpaths_2 compose
           (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x2 x3
              y f2) ((pr12 V) y x3) @
         assoc' (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x3 y)
           ((pr12 V) y x3) @
         maponpaths (compose (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
           (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x3 y)) @
         id_right (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) @
      ! bifunctor_rightcomp V y x1 x2 x3 f1 f2))
  (B xx1 yy ;; (Tl yy ff1 ;; Tl yy ff2) ;; B yy xx3) =

           (identity (y ⊗ x2) · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
           ((pr12 V) y x2 · (pr12 V) x2 y
            · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2) ((pr12 V) y x3)
           (cancel_postcomposition (identity (y ⊗ x2))
              ((pr12 V) y x2 · (pr12 V) x2 y)
              (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
              (! sym_mon_braiding_inv V y x2))) @
      maponpaths
        (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1))
        (cancel_postcomposition
           ((pr12 V) y x2 · (pr12 V) x2 y
            · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
           ((pr12 V) y x2
            · ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2))
           ((pr12 V) y x3)
           (! assoc ((pr12 V) y x2) ((pr12 V) x2 y)
                (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2))) @
      maponpaths
        (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1))
        (! assoc ((pr12 V) y x2)
             ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
             ((pr12 V) y x3)) @
      assoc ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1)
        ((pr12 V) y x2)
        ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2
         · (pr12 V) y x3) @
      cancel_postcomposition
        ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1
         · (pr12 V) y x2) (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)
        ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2
         · (pr12 V) y x3)
        (maponpaths_2 compose
           (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1 x2
              y f1) ((pr12 V) y x2) @
         assoc' (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x2 y)
           ((pr12 V) y x2) @
         maponpaths (compose (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
           (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x2 y)) @
         id_right (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) @
      maponpaths (compose (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
        (maponpaths_2 compose
           (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x2 x3
              y f2) ((pr12 V) y x3) @
         assoc' (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x3 y)
           ((pr12 V) y x3) @
         maponpaths (compose (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
           (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x3 y)) @
         id_right (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) @
      ! bifunctor_rightcomp V y x1 x2 x3 f1 f2))
  (transportb (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T yy xx3))
     (assoc ((pr12 V) x1 y) (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1)
        (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2))
     (B xx1 yy ;; Tl yy ff1 ;; Tl yy ff2) ;; B yy xx3) =
transportb (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx3 yy))
  (assoc ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1)
     (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2) ((pr12 V) y x3))
  (B xx1 yy ;; Tl yy ff1 ;; Tl yy ff2 ;; B yy xx3)

    
V: sym_monoidal_cat
D: disp_cat V
disp_tensor_ob: ∏ x y : V, D x → D y → D (x ⊗ y)
T:= λ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y), disp_tensor_ob x y xx yy: ∏ x y : V, D x → D y → D (x ⊗ y)
disp_lwhisker: ∏ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧)
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
(yy2 : D y2),
yy1 -->[ g] yy2
→ T xx yy1 -->[
  x ⊗^{ V}_{l} g] T xx yy2
Tl:= λ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧) 
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
(yy2 : D y2) (gg : yy1 -->[ g] yy2),
disp_lwhisker x y1 y2 g xx yy1 yy2 gg: ∏ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧) 
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
(yy2 : D y2),
yy1 -->[ g] yy2
→ T xx yy1 -->[ x ⊗^{ V}_{l} g] T xx yy2
disp_braiding: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
T xx yy -->[
sym_mon_braiding V x y] 
T yy xx
B:= λ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y), disp_braiding x y xx yy: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
T xx yy -->[ sym_mon_braiding V x y] T yy xx
Tr:= λ (x1 x2 y : V) (f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧) 
(xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2) 
(yy : D y) (ff : xx1 -->[ f] xx2),
let t := B xx1 yy ;; Tl yy ff ;; B yy xx2 in
transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx2 yy))
  (maponpaths_2 compose
     (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1 x2 y
        f) (sym_mon_braiding V y x2) @
   assoc' (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) 
     (V x2 y) (sym_mon_braiding V y x2) @
   maponpaths (compose (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
     (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x2 y)) @
   id_right (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) t: ∏ (x1 x2 y : V) (f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧) 
(xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2) 
(yy : D y),
xx1 -->[ f] xx2
→ T xx1 yy -->[ f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y] T xx2 yy
disp_lwhisker_preserves_id: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x)
(yy : D y),
Tl xx (id_disp yy) =
transportb
  (mor_disp (T xx yy)
     (T xx yy))
  (bifunctor_leftid V x y)
  (id_disp (T xx yy))
B_inv: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
B xx yy ;; B yy xx =
transportb (mor_disp (T xx yy) (T xx yy))
  (sym_mon_braiding_inv V x y)
  (id_disp (T xx yy))
disp_lwhisker_preserves_comp: ∏ (x y1 y2 y3 : V)
(g1 : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧)
(g2 : V ⟦ y2, y3 ⟧)
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1)
(yy2 : D y2)
(yy3 : D y3)
(gg1 : yy1 -->[ g1] yy2)
(gg2 : yy2 -->[ g2] yy3),
Tl xx (gg1 ;; gg2) =
transportb
  (mor_disp (T xx yy1)
     (T xx yy3))
  (bifunctor_leftcomp V
     x y1 y2 y3 g1 g2)
  (Tl xx gg1 ;; Tl xx
                  gg2)
x1, x2, x3, y: V
f1: V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧
f2: V ⟦ x2, x3 ⟧
xx1: D x1
xx2: D x2
xx3: D x3
yy: D y
ff1: xx1 -->[ f1] xx2
ff2: xx2 -->[ f2] xx3
transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx3 yy))
  ((cancel_postcomposition
      ((pr12 V) x1 y
       · (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1 · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2))
      ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} (f1 · f2))
      ((pr12 V) y x3)
      (maponpaths (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y))
         (! bifunctor_leftcomp V y x1 x2 x3 f1 f2)) @
    maponpaths_2 compose
      (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1 x3 y
         (f1 · f2)) ((pr12 V) y x3) @
    assoc' ((f1 · f2) ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x3 y)
      ((pr12 V) y x3) @
    maponpaths (compose ((f1 · f2) ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
      (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x3 y)) @
    id_right ((f1 · f2) ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) @
   ! (maponpaths
        (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1))
        (cancel_postcomposition (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
           (identity (y ⊗ x2) · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
           ((pr12 V) y x3)
           (! id_left (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2))) @
      maponpaths
        (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1))
        (cancel_postcomposition
           (identity (y ⊗ x2) · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
           ((pr12 V) y x2 · (pr12 V) x2 y
            · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2) ((pr12 V) y x3)
           (cancel_postcomposition (identity (y ⊗ x2))
              ((pr12 V) y x2 · (pr12 V) x2 y)
              (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
              (! sym_mon_braiding_inv V y x2))) @
      maponpaths
        (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1))
        (cancel_postcomposition
           ((pr12 V) y x2 · (pr12 V) x2 y
            · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
           ((pr12 V) y x2
            · ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2))
           ((pr12 V) y x3)
           (! assoc ((pr12 V) y x2) ((pr12 V) x2 y)
                (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2))) @
      maponpaths
        (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1))
        (! assoc ((pr12 V) y x2)
             ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
             ((pr12 V) y x3)) @
      assoc ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1)
        ((pr12 V) y x2)
        ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2
         · (pr12 V) y x3) @
      cancel_postcomposition
        ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1
         · (pr12 V) y x2) (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)
        ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2
         · (pr12 V) y x3)
        (maponpaths_2 compose
           (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1 x2
              y f1) ((pr12 V) y x2) @
         assoc' (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x2 y)
           ((pr12 V) y x2) @
         maponpaths (compose (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
           (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x2 y)) @
         id_right (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) @
      maponpaths (compose (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
        (maponpaths_2 compose
           (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x2 x3
              y f2) ((pr12 V) y x3) @
         assoc' (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x3 y)
           ((pr12 V) y x3) @
         maponpaths (compose (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
           (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x3 y)) @
         id_right (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) @
      ! bifunctor_rightcomp V y x1 x2 x3 f1 f2))
  (transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T yy xx3))
     (! assoc ((pr12 V) x1 y) (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1)
          (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2))
     (B xx1 yy ;; Tl yy ff1 ;; Tl yy ff2) ;; B yy xx3) =
transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx3 yy))
  (! assoc ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1)
       (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2) ((pr12 V) y x3))
  (B xx1 yy ;; Tl yy ff1 ;; Tl yy ff2 ;; B yy xx3)

      (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x3 y)) @
    id_right ((f1 · f2) ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) @
   ! (maponpaths
        (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1))

        (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1))

           (identity (y ⊗ x2) · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
           ((pr12 V) y x2 · (pr12 V) x2 y
            · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2) ((pr12 V) y x3)
           (cancel_postcomposition (identity (y ⊗ x2))
              ((pr12 V) y x2 · (pr12 V) x2 y)
              (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
              (! sym_mon_braiding_inv V y x2))) @

        (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1))

           ((pr12 V) y x2 · (pr12 V) x2 y
            · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
           ((pr12 V) y x2
            · ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2))
           ((pr12 V) y x3)
           (! assoc ((pr12 V) y x2) ((pr12 V) x2 y)
                (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2))) @
      maponpaths
        (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1))
        (! assoc ((pr12 V) y x2)
             ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
             ((pr12 V) y x3)) @
      assoc ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1)
        ((pr12 V) y x2)
        ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2
         · (pr12 V) y x3) @
      cancel_postcomposition
        ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1
         · (pr12 V) y x2) (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)
        ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2
         · (pr12 V) y x3)
        (maponpaths_2 compose
           (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1 x2
              y f1) ((pr12 V) y x2) @
         assoc' (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x2 y)
           ((pr12 V) y x2) @
         maponpaths (compose (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
           (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x2 y)) @
         id_right (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) @
      maponpaths (compose (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
        (maponpaths_2 compose
           (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x2 x3
              y f2) ((pr12 V) y x3) @
         assoc' (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x3 y)
           ((pr12 V) y x3) @
         maponpaths (compose (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
           (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x3 y)) @
         id_right (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) @
      ! bifunctor_rightcomp V y x1 x2 x3 f1 f2))
  (transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx3 yy))
     (cancel_postcomposition
        ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1
         · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
        ((pr12 V) x1 y
         · (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1 · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2))

        (! assoc ((pr12 V) x1 y) (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1)
             (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)))

(yy : D y),
