transportb (mor_disp (T xx yy) (T xx yy))
  (sym_mon_braiding_inv V x y)
  (id_disp (T xx yy))
disp_lwhisker_preserves_comp: ∏ (x y1 y2 y3 : V)
(g1 : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧)
(g2 : V ⟦ y2, y3 ⟧)
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1)
(yy2 : D y2)
(yy3 : D y3)
(gg1 : yy1 -->[ g1] yy2)
(gg2 : yy2 -->[ g2] yy3),
Tl xx (gg1 ;; gg2) =
transportb
  (mor_disp (T xx yy1)
     (T xx yy3))
  (bifunctor_leftcomp V
     x y1 y2 y3 g1 g2)
  (Tl xx gg1 ;; Tl xx
                  gg2)
x1, x2, x3, y: V
f1: V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧
f2: V ⟦ x2, x3 ⟧
xx1: D x1
xx2: D x2
xx3: D x3
yy: D y
ff1: xx1 -->[ f1] xx2
ff2: xx2 -->[ f2] xx3
transportb (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx3 yy))
  (! assoc ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1)
       (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2) ((pr12 V) y x3))
  (transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx3 yy))
     ((cancel_postcomposition
         ((pr12 V) x1 y
          · (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1 · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2))
         ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} (f1 · f2))
         ((pr12 V) y x3)
         (maponpaths (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y))
            (! bifunctor_leftcomp V y x1 x2 x3 f1 f2)) @
       maponpaths_2 compose
         (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1 x3 y
            (f1 · f2)) ((pr12 V) y x3) @
       assoc' ((f1 · f2) ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x3 y)
         ((pr12 V) y x3) @
       maponpaths (compose ((f1 · f2) ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
         (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x3 y)) @
       id_right ((f1 · f2) ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) @
      ! (maponpaths
           (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1))
           (cancel_postcomposition (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
              (identity (y ⊗ x2) · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
              ((pr12 V) y x3)
              (! id_left (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2))) @
         maponpaths
           (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1))
           (cancel_postcomposition
              (identity (y ⊗ x2) · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
              ((pr12 V) y x2 · (pr12 V) x2 y
               · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2) ((pr12 V) y x3)
              (cancel_postcomposition
                 (identity (y ⊗ x2))
                 ((pr12 V) y x2 · (pr12 V) x2 y)
                 (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
                 (! sym_mon_braiding_inv V y x2))) @
         maponpaths
           (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1))
           (cancel_postcomposition
              ((pr12 V) y x2 · (pr12 V) x2 y
               · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
              ((pr12 V) y x2
               · ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2))
              ((pr12 V) y x3)
              (! assoc ((pr12 V) y x2) ((pr12 V) x2 y)
                   (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2))) @
         maponpaths
           (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1))
           (! assoc ((pr12 V) y x2)
                ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
                ((pr12 V) y x3)) @
         assoc ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1)
           ((pr12 V) y x2)
           ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2
            · (pr12 V) y x3) @
         cancel_postcomposition
           ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1
            · (pr12 V) y x2) (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)
           ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2
            · (pr12 V) y x3)
           (maponpaths_2 compose
              (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1
                 x2 y f1) ((pr12 V) y x2) @
            assoc' (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x2 y)
              ((pr12 V) y x2) @
            maponpaths (compose (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
              (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x2 y)) @
            id_right (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) @
         maponpaths (compose (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
           (maponpaths_2 compose
              (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x2
                 x3 y f2) ((pr12 V) y x3) @
            assoc' (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x3 y)
              ((pr12 V) y x3) @
            maponpaths (compose (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
              (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x3 y)) @
            id_right (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) @
         ! bifunctor_rightcomp V y x1 x2 x3 f1 f2))
     (transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx3 yy))
        (cancel_postcomposition
           ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1
            · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
           ((pr12 V) x1 y
            · (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1 · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2))
           ((pr12 V) y x3)
           (! assoc ((pr12 V) x1 y) (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1)
                (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)))
        (B xx1 yy ;; Tl yy ff1 ;; Tl yy ff2 ;; B yy
                                                 xx3))) =
B xx1 yy ;; Tl yy ff1 ;; Tl yy ff2 ;; B yy xx3

    
V: sym_monoidal_cat
D: disp_cat V
disp_tensor_ob: ∏ x y : V, D x → D y → D (x ⊗ y)
T:= λ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y), disp_tensor_ob x y xx yy: ∏ x y : V, D x → D y → D (x ⊗ y)
disp_lwhisker: ∏ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧)
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
(yy2 : D y2),
yy1 -->[ g] yy2
→ T xx yy1 -->[
  x ⊗^{ V}_{l} g] T xx yy2
Tl:= λ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧) 
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
(yy2 : D y2) (gg : yy1 -->[ g] yy2),
disp_lwhisker x y1 y2 g xx yy1 yy2 gg: ∏ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧)

(yy2 : D y2),

→ T xx yy1 -->[ x ⊗^{ V}_{l} g] T xx yy2
disp_braiding: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
T xx yy -->[
sym_mon_braiding V x y] 
T yy xx
B:= λ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y), disp_braiding x y xx yy: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
T xx yy -->[ sym_mon_braiding V x y] T yy xx
Tr:= λ (x1 x2 y : V) (f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧) 
(xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2) 
(yy : D y) (ff : xx1 -->[ f] xx2),
let t := B xx1 yy ;; Tl yy ff ;; B yy xx2 in
transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx2 yy))
  (maponpaths_2 compose
     (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1 x2 y
        f) (sym_mon_braiding V y x2) @
   assoc' (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) 
     (V x2 y) (sym_mon_braiding V y x2) @
   maponpaths (compose (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
     (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x2 y)) @
   id_right (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) t: ∏ (x1 x2 y : V) (f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧) 
(xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2) 
(yy : D y),
xx1 -->[ f] xx2
→ T xx1 yy -->[ f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y] T xx2 yy
disp_lwhisker_preserves_id: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x)
(yy : D y),

transportb
  (mor_disp (T xx yy)
     (T xx yy))
  (bifunctor_leftid V x y)
  (id_disp (T xx yy))

  (sym_mon_braiding_inv V x y)
  (id_disp (T xx yy))

              ((pr12 V) y x2 · (pr12 V) x2 y

              ((pr12 V) y x2 · (pr12 V) x2 y

               · ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2))

           (! assoc ((pr12 V) y x2)
                ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
                ((pr12 V) y x3)) @
         assoc ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1)
           ((pr12 V) y x2)
           ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2
            · (pr12 V) y x3) @
         cancel_postcomposition
           ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1
            · (pr12 V) y x2) (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)
           ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2
            · (pr12 V) y x3)
           (maponpaths_2 compose
              (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1
                 x2 y f1) ((pr12 V) y x2) @

              ((pr12 V) y x3) @
            maponpaths (compose (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))

            id_right (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) @

     (transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx3 yy))
        (cancel_postcomposition
           ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1
            · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
           ((pr12 V) x1 y
            · (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1 · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2))
           ((pr12 V) y x3)

                                                 xx3))) =

disp_lwhisker_preserves_comp: ∏ (x y1 y2 y3 : V)
(g1 : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧)
(g2 : V ⟦ y2, y3 ⟧)
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1)
(yy2 : D y2)

x1, x2, x3, y: V
f1: V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧
f2: V ⟦ x2, x3 ⟧
xx1: D x1
xx2: D x2
xx3: D x3
yy: D y
ff1: xx1 -->[ f1] xx2
ff2: xx2 -->[ f2] xx3
transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx3 yy))
  (cancel_postcomposition
     ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1
      · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
     ((pr12 V) x1 y
      · (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1 · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2))
     ((pr12 V) y x3)
     (! assoc ((pr12 V) x1 y) (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1)
          (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)) @
   ((cancel_postcomposition
       ((pr12 V) x1 y
        · (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1 · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2))
       ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} (f1 · f2))
       ((pr12 V) y x3)
       (maponpaths (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y))
          (! bifunctor_leftcomp V y x1 x2 x3 f1 f2)) @
     maponpaths_2 compose
       (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1 x3 y
          (f1 · f2)) ((pr12 V) y x3) @
     assoc' ((f1 · f2) ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x3 y)
       ((pr12 V) y x3) @
     maponpaths (compose ((f1 · f2) ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
       (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x3 y)) @
     id_right ((f1 · f2) ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) @
    ! (maponpaths
         (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1))
         (cancel_postcomposition (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
            (identity (y ⊗ x2) · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
            ((pr12 V) y x3)
            (! id_left (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2))) @
       maponpaths
         (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1))
         (cancel_postcomposition
            (identity (y ⊗ x2) · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
            ((pr12 V) y x2 · (pr12 V) x2 y
             · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2) ((pr12 V) y x3)
            (cancel_postcomposition
               (identity (y ⊗ x2))
               ((pr12 V) y x2 · (pr12 V) x2 y)
               (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
               (! sym_mon_braiding_inv V y x2))) @
       maponpaths
         (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1))
         (cancel_postcomposition
            ((pr12 V) y x2 · (pr12 V) x2 y
             · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
            ((pr12 V) y x2
             · ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2))
            ((pr12 V) y x3)
            (! assoc ((pr12 V) y x2) ((pr12 V) x2 y)
                 (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2))) @
       maponpaths
         (compose ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1))
         (! assoc ((pr12 V) y x2)
              ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2)
              ((pr12 V) y x3)) @
       assoc ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1)
         ((pr12 V) y x2)
         ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2
          · (pr12 V) y x3) @
       cancel_postcomposition
         ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1
          · (pr12 V) y x2) (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)
         ((pr12 V) x2 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2
          · (pr12 V) y x3)
         (maponpaths_2 compose
            (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1
               x2 y f1) ((pr12 V) y x2) @
          assoc' (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x2 y)
            ((pr12 V) y x2) @
          maponpaths (compose (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
            (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x2 y)) @
          id_right (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) @
       maponpaths (compose (f1 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
         (maponpaths_2 compose
            (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x2
               x3 y f2) ((pr12 V) y x3) @
          assoc' (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) (pr1 V x3 y)
            ((pr12 V) y x3) @
          maponpaths (compose (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
            (pr1 ((pr122 (...)) x3 y)) @
          id_right (f2 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) @
       ! bifunctor_rightcomp V y x1 x2 x3 f1 f2)) @
   ! (! assoc ((pr12 V) x1 y · y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f1)
          (y ⊗^{ V}_{l} f2) ((pr12 V) y x3)))
  (B xx1 yy ;; Tl yy ff1 ;; Tl yy ff2 ;; B yy xx3) =
B xx1 yy ;; Tl yy ff1 ;; Tl yy ff2 ;; B yy xx3

    
V: sym_monoidal_cat
D: disp_cat V
disp_tensor_ob: ∏ x y : V, D x → D y → D (x ⊗ y)
T:= λ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y), disp_tensor_ob x y xx yy: ∏ x y : V, D x → D y → D (x ⊗ y)
disp_lwhisker: ∏ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧)
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
(yy2 : D y2),
yy1 -->[ g] yy2
→ T xx yy1 -->[
  x ⊗^{ V}_{l} g] T xx yy2
Tl:= λ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧) 
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
(yy2 : D y2) (gg : yy1 -->[ g] yy2),
disp_lwhisker x y1 y2 g xx yy1 yy2 gg: ∏ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧) 
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
(yy2 : D y2),
yy1 -->[ g] yy2
→ T xx yy1 -->[ x ⊗^{ V}_{l} g] T xx yy2
disp_braiding: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
T xx yy -->[
sym_mon_braiding V x y] 
T yy xx
B:= λ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y), disp_braiding x y xx yy: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
T xx yy -->[ sym_mon_braiding V x y] T yy xx
Tr:= λ (x1 x2 y : V) (f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧) 
(xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2) 
(yy : D y) (ff : xx1 -->[ f] xx2),
let t := B xx1 yy ;; Tl yy ff ;; B yy xx2 in
transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx2 yy))
  (maponpaths_2 compose
     (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1 x2 y
        f) (sym_mon_braiding V y x2) @
   assoc' (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) 
     (V x2 y) (sym_mon_braiding V y x2) @
   maponpaths (compose (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
     (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x2 y)) @
   id_right (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) t: ∏ (x1 x2 y : V) (f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧) 
(xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2) 
(yy : D y),
xx1 -->[ f] xx2
→ T xx1 yy -->[ f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y] T xx2 yy
disp_lwhisker_preserves_id: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x)
(yy : D y),
Tl xx (id_disp yy) =
transportb
  (mor_disp (T xx yy)
     (T xx yy))
  (bifunctor_leftid V x y)
  (id_disp (T xx yy))
B_inv: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
B xx yy ;; B yy xx =
transportb (mor_disp (T xx yy) (T xx yy))
  (sym_mon_braiding_inv V x y)
  (id_disp (T xx yy))
disp_lwhisker_preserves_comp: ∏ (x y1 y2 y3 : V)
(g1 : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧)
(g2 : V ⟦ y2, y3 ⟧)
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1)
(yy2 : D y2)
(yy3 : D y3)
(gg1 : yy1 -->[ g1] yy2)
(gg2 : yy2 -->[ g2] yy3),
Tl xx (gg1 ;; gg2) =
transportb
  (mor_disp (T xx yy1)
     (T xx yy3))
  (bifunctor_leftcomp V
     x y1 y2 y3 g1 g2)
  (Tl xx gg1 ;; Tl xx
                  gg2)
x1, x2, x3, y: V
f1: V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧
f2: V ⟦ x2, x3 ⟧
xx1: D x1
xx2: D x2
xx3: D x3
yy: D y
ff1: xx1 -->[ f1] xx2
ff2: xx2 -->[ f2] xx3
isaset (V ⟦ x1 ⊗ y, x3 ⊗ y ⟧)

    apply homset_property.
  Qed.

  (* Lemma B_naturality
    : B x1 y1 xx1 yy1 ;; Tl yy1 ff = Tl _ ff *)

  Context (disp_tensor_equalwhiskers
            : ∏ (x1 x2 y1 y2 : V) (f : V⟦ x1, x2 ⟧) (g : V⟦ y1, y2 ⟧)
                (xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2) (yy1 : D y1) (yy2 : D y2)
                (ff : xx1 -->[ f] xx2) (gg : yy1 -->[ g] yy2),
              Tr yy1 ff ;; Tl xx2 gg
              = transportb _ (bifunctor_equalwhiskers V x1 x2 y1 y2 f g)
                  (Tl xx1 gg ;; Tr yy2 ff)).

  x ⊗^{ V}_{l} g] T xx yy2

(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
(yy2 : D y2) (gg : yy1 -->[ g] yy2),
disp_lwhisker x y1 y2 g xx yy1 yy2 gg: ∏ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧) 
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
(yy2 : D y2),
yy1 -->[ g] yy2
→ T xx yy1 -->[ x ⊗^{ V}_{l} g] T xx yy2
disp_braiding: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
T xx yy -->[
sym_mon_braiding V x y] 
T yy xx
B:= λ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y), disp_braiding x y xx yy: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
T xx yy -->[ sym_mon_braiding V x y] T yy xx
Tr:= λ (x1 x2 y : V) (f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧) 
(xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2) 
(yy : D y) (ff : xx1 -->[ f] xx2),
let t := B xx1 yy ;; Tl yy ff ;; B yy xx2 in
transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx2 yy))
  (maponpaths_2 compose
     (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1 x2 y
        f) (sym_mon_braiding V y x2) @
   assoc' (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) 
     (V x2 y) (sym_mon_braiding V y x2) @
   maponpaths (compose (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
     (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x2 y)) @
   id_right (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) t: ∏ (x1 x2 y : V) (f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧) 
(xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2) 
(yy : D y),
xx1 -->[ f] xx2
→ T xx1 yy -->[ f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y] T xx2 yy
disp_lwhisker_preserves_id: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x)
(yy : D y),
Tl xx (id_disp yy) =
transportb
  (mor_disp (T xx yy)
     (T xx yy))
  (bifunctor_leftid V x y)
  (id_disp (T xx yy))
B_inv: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
B xx yy ;; B yy xx =
transportb (mor_disp (T xx yy) (T xx yy))
  (sym_mon_braiding_inv V x y)
  (id_disp (T xx yy))
disp_lwhisker_preserves_comp: ∏ (x y1 y2 y3 : V)
(g1 : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧)
(g2 : V ⟦ y2, y3 ⟧)
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1)
(yy2 : D y2)
(yy3 : D y3)
(gg1 : yy1 -->[ g1] yy2)
(gg2 : yy2 -->[ g2] yy3),
Tl xx (gg1 ;; gg2) =
transportb
  (mor_disp (T xx yy1)
     (T xx yy3))
  (bifunctor_leftcomp V
     x y1 y2 y3 g1 g2)
  (Tl xx gg1 ;; Tl xx
                  gg2)
disp_tensor_equalwhiskers: ∏ (x1 x2 y1 y2 : V)
(f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧)
(g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧)
(xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2)
(yy1 : D y1) (yy2 : D y2)
(ff : xx1 -->[ f] xx2)
(gg : yy1 -->[ g] yy2),
Tr yy1 ff ;; Tl xx2 gg =
transportb
  (mor_disp (T xx1 yy1)
     (T xx2 yy2))
  (bifunctor_equalwhiskers
     V x1 x2 y1 y2 f g)
  (Tl xx1 gg ;; Tr yy2 ff)

         x ⊗^{ V}_{l} g] 
         ?pr1 x y2 xx yy2,

(yy : D y), disp_braiding x y xx yy: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
T xx yy -->[ sym_mon_braiding V x y] T yy xx
Tr:= λ (x1 x2 y : V) (f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧) 
(xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2) 
(yy : D y) (ff : xx1 -->[ f] xx2),
let t := B xx1 yy ;; Tl yy ff ;; B yy xx2 in
transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx2 yy))
  (maponpaths_2 compose
     (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1 x2 y
        f) (sym_mon_braiding V y x2) @
   assoc' (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) 
     (V x2 y) (sym_mon_braiding V y x2) @
   maponpaths (compose (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
     (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x2 y)) @
   id_right (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) t: ∏ (x1 x2 y : V) (f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧) 
(xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2) 
(yy : D y),
xx1 -->[ f] xx2
→ T xx1 yy -->[ f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y] T xx2 yy
disp_lwhisker_preserves_id: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x)
(yy : D y),
Tl xx (id_disp yy) =
transportb
  (mor_disp (T xx yy)
     (T xx yy))
  (bifunctor_leftid V x y)
  (id_disp (T xx yy))

(yy : D y),
B xx yy ;; B yy xx =

  (sym_mon_braiding_inv V x y)
  (id_disp (T xx yy))
disp_lwhisker_preserves_comp: ∏ (x y1 y2 y3 : V)
(g1 : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧)
(g2 : V ⟦ y2, y3 ⟧)
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1)
(yy2 : D y2)
(yy3 : D y3)

     (T xx2 yy2))

     V x1 x2 y1 y2 f g)
  (Tl xx1 gg ;; Tr yy2 ff)

V: sym_monoidal_cat
D: disp_cat V
disp_tensor_ob: ∏ x y : V, D x → D y → D (x ⊗ y)
T:= λ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y), disp_tensor_ob x y xx yy: ∏ x y : V, D x → D y → D (x ⊗ y)
disp_lwhisker: ∏ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧)
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
(yy2 : D y2),
yy1 -->[ g] yy2
→ T xx yy1 -->[
  x ⊗^{ V}_{l} g] T xx yy2
Tl:= λ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧) 
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
(yy2 : D y2) (gg : yy1 -->[ g] yy2),
disp_lwhisker x y1 y2 g xx yy1 yy2 gg: ∏ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧) 
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
(yy2 : D y2),
yy1 -->[ g] yy2
→ T xx yy1 -->[ x ⊗^{ V}_{l} g] T xx yy2
disp_braiding: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
T xx yy -->[
sym_mon_braiding V x y] 
T yy xx
B:= λ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y), disp_braiding x y xx yy: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
T xx yy -->[ sym_mon_braiding V x y] T yy xx
Tr:= λ (x1 x2 y : V) (f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧) 
(xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2) 
(yy : D y) (ff : xx1 -->[ f] xx2),
let t := B xx1 yy ;; Tl yy ff ;; B yy xx2 in
transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx2 yy))
  (maponpaths_2 compose
     (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1 x2 y
        f) (sym_mon_braiding V y x2) @
   assoc' (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) 
     (V x2 y) (sym_mon_braiding V y x2) @
   maponpaths (compose (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
     (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x2 y)) @
   id_right (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) t: ∏ (x1 x2 y : V) (f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧) 
(xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2) 
(yy : D y),
xx1 -->[ f] xx2
→ T xx1 yy -->[ f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y] T xx2 yy
disp_lwhisker_preserves_id: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x)
(yy : D y),
Tl xx (id_disp yy) =
transportb
  (mor_disp (T xx yy)
     (T xx yy))
  (bifunctor_leftid V x y)
  (id_disp (T xx yy))
B_inv: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
B xx yy ;; B yy xx =
transportb (mor_disp (T xx yy) (T xx yy))
  (sym_mon_braiding_inv V x y)
  (id_disp (T xx yy))
disp_lwhisker_preserves_comp: ∏ (x y1 y2 y3 : V)
(g1 : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧)
(g2 : V ⟦ y2, y3 ⟧)
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1)
(yy2 : D y2)
(yy3 : D y3)
(gg1 : yy1 -->[ g1] yy2)
(gg2 : yy2 -->[ g2] yy3),
Tl xx (gg1 ;; gg2) =
transportb
  (mor_disp (T xx yy1)
     (T xx yy3))
  (bifunctor_leftcomp V
     x y1 y2 y3 g1 g2)
  (Tl xx gg1 ;; Tl xx
                  gg2)
disp_tensor_equalwhiskers: ∏ (x1 x2 y1 y2 : V)
(f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧)
(g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧)
(xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2)
(yy1 : D y1) (yy2 : D y2)
(ff : xx1 -->[ f] xx2)
(gg : yy1 -->[ g] yy2),
Tr yy1 ff ;; Tl xx2 gg =
transportb
  (mor_disp (T xx1 yy1)
     (T xx2 yy2))
  (bifunctor_equalwhiskers
     V x1 x2 y1 y2 f g)
  (Tl xx1 gg ;; Tr yy2 ff)
II: D I_{ V}
lu_lu: disp_leftunitor_data
  make_symmetric_monoidal_disp_cat_tensor II
lu_lu_inv: disp_leftunitorinv_data
  make_symmetric_monoidal_disp_cat_tensor
  II
x: V
xx: D x
T xx II -->[ mon_runitor x] xx

  Defined.

  Context (asas : disp_associator_data make_symmetric_monoidal_disp_cat_tensor).
  Context (asasinv : disp_associatorinv_data make_symmetric_monoidal_disp_cat_tensor).

  
V: sym_monoidal_cat
D: disp_cat V
disp_tensor_ob: ∏ x y : V, D x → D y → D (x ⊗ y)
T:= λ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y), disp_tensor_ob x y xx yy: ∏ x y : V, D x → D y → D (x ⊗ y)
disp_lwhisker: ∏ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧)
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
(yy2 : D y2),
yy1 -->[ g] yy2
→ T xx yy1 -->[
  x ⊗^{ V}_{l} g] T xx yy2
Tl:= λ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧) 
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
(yy2 : D y2) (gg : yy1 -->[ g] yy2),
disp_lwhisker x y1 y2 g xx yy1 yy2 gg: ∏ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧) 
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
(yy2 : D y2),
yy1 -->[ g] yy2
→ T xx yy1 -->[ x ⊗^{ V}_{l} g] T xx yy2
disp_braiding: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
T xx yy -->[
sym_mon_braiding V x y] 
T yy xx
B:= λ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y), disp_braiding x y xx yy: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
T xx yy -->[ sym_mon_braiding V x y] T yy xx
Tr:= λ (x1 x2 y : V) (f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧) 
(xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2) 
(yy : D y) (ff : xx1 -->[ f] xx2),
let t := B xx1 yy ;; Tl yy ff ;; B yy xx2 in
transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx2 yy))
  (maponpaths_2 compose
     (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1 x2 y
        f) (sym_mon_braiding V y x2) @
   assoc' (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) 
     (V x2 y) (sym_mon_braiding V y x2) @
   maponpaths (compose (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
     (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x2 y)) @
   id_right (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) t: ∏ (x1 x2 y : V) (f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧) 
(xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2) 
(yy : D y),
xx1 -->[ f] xx2
→ T xx1 yy -->[ f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y] T xx2 yy
disp_lwhisker_preserves_id: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x)
(yy : D y),
Tl xx (id_disp yy) =
transportb
  (mor_disp (T xx yy)
     (T xx yy))
  (bifunctor_leftid V x y)
  (id_disp (T xx yy))
B_inv: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
B xx yy ;; B yy xx =
transportb (mor_disp (T xx yy) (T xx yy))
  (sym_mon_braiding_inv V x y)
  (id_disp (T xx yy))
disp_lwhisker_preserves_comp: ∏ (x y1 y2 y3 : V)
(g1 : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧)
(g2 : V ⟦ y2, y3 ⟧)
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1)
(yy2 : D y2)
(yy3 : D y3)
(gg1 : yy1 -->[ g1] yy2)
(gg2 : yy2 -->[ g2] yy3),
Tl xx (gg1 ;; gg2) =
transportb
  (mor_disp (T xx yy1)
     (T xx yy3))
  (bifunctor_leftcomp V
     x y1 y2 y3 g1 g2)
  (Tl xx gg1 ;; Tl xx
                  gg2)
disp_tensor_equalwhiskers: ∏ (x1 x2 y1 y2 : V)
(f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧)
(g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧)
(xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2)
(yy1 : D y1) (yy2 : D y2)
(ff : xx1 -->[ f] xx2)
(gg : yy1 -->[ g] yy2),
Tr yy1 ff ;; Tl xx2 gg =
transportb
  (mor_disp (T xx1 yy1)
     (T xx2 yy2))
  (bifunctor_equalwhiskers
     V x1 x2 y1 y2 f g)
  (Tl xx1 gg ;; Tr yy2 ff)
II: D I_{ V}
lu_lu: disp_leftunitor_data
  make_symmetric_monoidal_disp_cat_tensor II
lu_lu_inv: disp_leftunitorinv_data
  make_symmetric_monoidal_disp_cat_tensor
  II

(xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2)

transportb
  (mor_disp (T xx yy1)
     (T xx yy3))
  (bifunctor_leftcomp V
     x y1 y2 y3 g1 g2)
  (Tl xx gg1 ;; Tl xx
                  gg2)
disp_tensor_equalwhiskers: ∏ (x1 x2 y1 y2 : V)
(f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧)
(g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧)
(xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2)
(yy1 : D y1) (yy2 : D y2)
(ff : xx1 -->[ f] xx2)
(gg : yy1 -->[ g] yy2),
Tr yy1 ff ;; Tl xx2 gg =
transportb
  (mor_disp (T xx1 yy1)
     (T xx2 yy2))
  (bifunctor_equalwhiskers
     V x1 x2 y1 y2 f g)
  (Tl xx1 gg ;; Tr yy2 ff)

V: sym_monoidal_cat
D: disp_cat V
disp_tensor_ob: ∏ x y : V, D x → D y → D (x ⊗ y)
T:= λ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y), disp_tensor_ob x y xx yy: ∏ x y : V, D x → D y → D (x ⊗ y)
disp_lwhisker: ∏ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧)
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
(yy2 : D y2),
yy1 -->[ g] yy2
→ T xx yy1 -->[
  x ⊗^{ V}_{l} g] T xx yy2
Tl:= λ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧) 
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
(yy2 : D y2) (gg : yy1 -->[ g] yy2),
disp_lwhisker x y1 y2 g xx yy1 yy2 gg: ∏ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧) 
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
(yy2 : D y2),
yy1 -->[ g] yy2
→ T xx yy1 -->[ x ⊗^{ V}_{l} g] T xx yy2
disp_braiding: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
T xx yy -->[
sym_mon_braiding V x y] 
T yy xx
B:= λ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y), disp_braiding x y xx yy: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
T xx yy -->[ sym_mon_braiding V x y] T yy xx
Tr:= λ (x1 x2 y : V) (f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧) 
(xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2) 
(yy : D y) (ff : xx1 -->[ f] xx2),
let t := B xx1 yy ;; Tl yy ff ;; B yy xx2 in
transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx2 yy))
  (maponpaths_2 compose
     (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1 x2 y
        f) (sym_mon_braiding V y x2) @
   assoc' (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) 
     (V x2 y) (sym_mon_braiding V y x2) @
   maponpaths (compose (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
     (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x2 y)) @
   id_right (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) t: ∏ (x1 x2 y : V) (f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧) 
(xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2) 
(yy : D y),
xx1 -->[ f] xx2
→ T xx1 yy -->[ f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y] T xx2 yy
disp_lwhisker_preserves_id: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x)
(yy : D y),
Tl xx (id_disp yy) =
transportb
  (mor_disp (T xx yy)
     (T xx yy))
  (bifunctor_leftid V x y)
  (id_disp (T xx yy))
B_inv: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
B xx yy ;; B yy xx =
transportb (mor_disp (T xx yy) (T xx yy))
  (sym_mon_braiding_inv V x y)
  (id_disp (T xx yy))
disp_lwhisker_preserves_comp: ∏ (x y1 y2 y3 : V)
(g1 : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧)
(g2 : V ⟦ y2, y3 ⟧)
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1)
(yy2 : D y2)
(yy3 : D y3)
(gg1 : yy1 -->[ g1] yy2)
(gg2 : yy2 -->[ g2] yy3),
Tl xx (gg1 ;; gg2) =
transportb
  (mor_disp (T xx yy1)
     (T xx yy3))
  (bifunctor_leftcomp V
     x y1 y2 y3 g1 g2)
  (Tl xx gg1 ;; Tl xx
                  gg2)
disp_tensor_equalwhiskers: ∏ (x1 x2 y1 y2 : V)
(f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧)
(g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧)
(xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2)
(yy1 : D y1) (yy2 : D y2)
(ff : xx1 -->[ f] xx2)
(gg : yy1 -->[ g] yy2),

   maponpaths (compose (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
     (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x2 y)) @
   id_right (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) t: ∏ (x1 x2 y : V) (f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧) 
(xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2) 
(yy : D y),
xx1 -->[ f] xx2
→ T xx1 yy -->[ f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y] T xx2 yy
disp_lwhisker_preserves_id: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x)
(yy : D y),
Tl xx (id_disp yy) =
transportb
  (mor_disp (T xx yy)
     (T xx yy))
  (bifunctor_leftid V x y)
  (id_disp (T xx yy))
B_inv: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
B xx yy ;; B yy xx =
transportb (mor_disp (T xx yy) (T xx yy))
  (sym_mon_braiding_inv V x y)
  (id_disp (T xx yy))
disp_lwhisker_preserves_comp: ∏ (x y1 y2 y3 : V)
(g1 : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧)
(g2 : V ⟦ y2, y3 ⟧)
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1)
(yy2 : D y2)
(yy3 : D y3)
(gg1 : yy1 -->[ g1] yy2)
(gg2 : yy2 -->[ g2] yy3),
Tl xx (gg1 ;; gg2) =
transportb
  (mor_disp (T xx yy1)
     (T xx yy3))
  (bifunctor_leftcomp V
     x y1 y2 y3 g1 g2)
  (Tl xx gg1 ;; Tl xx
                  gg2)
disp_tensor_equalwhiskers: ∏ (x1 x2 y1 y2 : V)
(f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧)
(g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧)
(xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2)
(yy1 : D y1) (yy2 : D y2)
(ff : xx1 -->[ f] xx2)
(gg : yy1 -->[ g] yy2),
Tr yy1 ff ;; Tl xx2 gg =
transportb
  (mor_disp (T xx1 yy1)
     (T xx2 yy2))
  (bifunctor_equalwhiskers
     V x1 x2 y1 y2 f g)
  (Tl xx1 gg ;; Tr yy2 ff)

disp_tensor_ob: ∏ x y : V, D x → D y → D (x ⊗ y)
T:= λ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y), disp_tensor_ob x y xx yy: ∏ x y : V, D x → D y → D (x ⊗ y)
disp_lwhisker: ∏ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧)
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
(yy2 : D y2),
yy1 -->[ g] yy2
→ T xx yy1 -->[
  x ⊗^{ V}_{l} g] T xx yy2
Tl:= λ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧) 
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
(yy2 : D y2) (gg : yy1 -->[ g] yy2),
disp_lwhisker x y1 y2 g xx yy1 yy2 gg: ∏ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧) 
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
(yy2 : D y2),
yy1 -->[ g] yy2
→ T xx yy1 -->[ x ⊗^{ V}_{l} g] T xx yy2
disp_braiding: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
T xx yy -->[
sym_mon_braiding V x y] 
T yy xx
B:= λ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y), disp_braiding x y xx yy: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
T xx yy -->[ sym_mon_braiding V x y] T yy xx
Tr:= λ (x1 x2 y : V) (f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧) 
(xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2) 
(yy : D y) (ff : xx1 -->[ f] xx2),
let t := B xx1 yy ;; Tl yy ff ;; B yy xx2 in
transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx2 yy))
  (maponpaths_2 compose
     (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1 x2 y
        f) (sym_mon_braiding V y x2) @
   assoc' (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) 
     (V x2 y) (sym_mon_braiding V y x2) @
   maponpaths (compose (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
     (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x2 y)) @
   id_right (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) t: ∏ (x1 x2 y : V) (f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧) 
(xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2) 
(yy : D y),
xx1 -->[ f] xx2
→ T xx1 yy -->[ f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y] T xx2 yy

(yy : D y),

(xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2) 
(yy : D y) (ff : xx1 -->[ f] xx2),
let t := B xx1 yy ;; Tl yy ff ;; B yy xx2 in
transportf (mor_disp (T xx1 yy) (T xx2 yy))
  (maponpaths_2 compose
     (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x1 x2 y
        f) (sym_mon_braiding V y x2) @
   assoc' (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) 
     (V x2 y) (sym_mon_braiding V y x2) @
   maponpaths (compose (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
     (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x2 y)) @
   id_right (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) t: ∏ (x1 x2 y : V) (f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧) 
(xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2) 
(yy : D y),
xx1 -->[ f] xx2
→ T xx1 yy -->[ f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y] T xx2 yy
disp_lwhisker_preserves_id: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x)
(yy : D y),
Tl xx (id_disp yy) =
transportb
  (mor_disp (T xx yy)
     (T xx yy))
  (bifunctor_leftid V x y)
  (id_disp (T xx yy))
B_inv: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y),
B xx yy ;; B yy xx =
transportb (mor_disp (T xx yy) (T xx yy))
  (sym_mon_braiding_inv V x y)
  (id_disp (T xx yy))
disp_lwhisker_preserves_comp: ∏ (x y1 y2 y3 : V)
(g1 : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧)
(g2 : V ⟦ y2, y3 ⟧)
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1)
(yy2 : D y2)
(yy3 : D y3)
(gg1 : yy1 -->[ g1] yy2)
(gg2 : yy2 -->[ g2] yy3),
Tl xx (gg1 ;; gg2) =
transportb
  (mor_disp (T xx yy1)
     (T xx yy3))
  (bifunctor_leftcomp V
     x y1 y2 y3 g1 g2)
  (Tl xx gg1 ;; Tl xx
                  gg2)
disp_tensor_equalwhiskers: ∏ (x1 x2 y1 y2 : V)
(f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧)
(g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧)
(xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2)
(yy1 : D y1) (yy2 : D y2)
(ff : xx1 -->[ f] xx2)
(gg : yy1 -->[ g] yy2),
Tr yy1 ff ;; Tl xx2 gg =

  (mor_disp (T xx1 yy1)
     (T xx2 yy2))
  (bifunctor_equalwhiskers
     V x1 x2 y1 y2 f g)
  (Tl xx1 gg ;; Tr yy2 ff)

(yy : D y) (zz : D z),

                        (y ⊗ z) xx
                        (T y z yy zz)

V: sym_monoidal_cat
D: disp_cat V
LP: locally_propositional D
T: ∏ x y : V, D x → D y → D (x ⊗ y)
Tmor: ∏ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧)

→ T x y1 xx yy1 -->[
  x ⊗^{ V}_{l} g] T x y2 xx yy2

lu_lu: ∏ (x : V) (xx : D x),

lu_lu_inv: ∏ (x : V) (xx : D x),

                        (y ⊗ z) xx
                        (T y z yy zz)

T x (y ⊗ z) xx (T y z yy zz) -->[
mon_rassociator x y z] T (x ⊗ y) z
                        (T x y xx yy) zz
∏ (x1 x2 y1 y2 : V) (f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧)
(g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧) (xx1 : D x1) 
(xx2 : D x2) (yy1 : D y1) 
(yy2 : D y2) (ff : xx1 -->[ f] xx2)
(gg : yy1 -->[ g] yy2),
(λ (x3 x4 y : V) (f0 : V ⟦ x3, x4 ⟧) 
 (xx3 : D x3) (xx4 : D x4) 
 (yy : D y) (ff0 : xx3 -->[ f0] xx4),
 let t :=
   (λ (x y0 : V) (xx : D x) 
    (yy0 : D y0), B x y0 xx yy0) x3 y xx3 yy ;; 
   (λ (x y3 y4 : V) (g0 : V ⟦ y3, y4 ⟧) 
    (xx : D x) (yy3 : D y3) 
    (yy4 : D y4) (gg0 : yy3 -->[ g0] yy4),
    Tmor x y3 y4 g0 xx yy3 yy4 gg0) y x3 x4 f0 yy xx3
     xx4 ff0 ;; (λ (x y0 : V) 
                 (xx : D x) 
                 (yy0 : D y0), 
                 B x y0 xx yy0) y x4 yy xx4 in
 transportf
   (mor_disp
      ((λ (x y0 : V) (xx : D x) 
        (yy0 : D y0), T x y0 xx yy0) x3 y xx3 yy)
      ((λ (x y0 : V) (xx : D x) 
        (yy0 : D y0), T x y0 xx yy0) x4 y xx4 yy))
   (maponpaths_2 compose
      (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V x3 x4 y f0)
      (sym_mon_braiding V y x4) @
    assoc' (f0 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y) 
      (V x4 y) (sym_mon_braiding V y x4) @
    maponpaths (compose (f0 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y))
      (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x4 y)) @
    id_right (f0 ⊗^{ V}_{r} y)) t) x1 x2 y1 f xx1 xx2
  yy1 ff ;; (λ (x y3 y4 : V) 
             (g0 : V ⟦ y3, y4 ⟧) 
             (xx : D x) (yy3 : D y3) 
             (yy4 : D y4) 
             (gg0 : yy3 -->[ g0] yy4),
             Tmor x y3 y4 g0 xx yy3 yy4 gg0) x2 y1 y2
              g xx2 yy1 yy2 gg =
transportb
  (mor_disp
     ((λ (x y : V) (xx : D x) (yy : D y), T x y xx yy)
        x1 y1 xx1 yy1)
     ((λ (x y : V) (xx : D x) (yy : D y), T x y xx yy)
        x2 y2 xx2 yy2))
  (bifunctor_equalwhiskers V x1 x2 y1 y2 f g)
  ((λ (x y3 y4 : V) (g0 : V ⟦ y3, y4 ⟧) 
    (xx : D x) (yy3 : D y3) 
    (yy4 : D y4) (gg0 : yy3 -->[ g0] yy4),
    Tmor x y3 y4 g0 xx yy3 yy4 gg0) x1 y1 y2 g xx1 yy1
     yy2 gg ;; (λ (x3 x4 y : V) 
                (f0 : V ⟦ x3, x4 ⟧) 
                (xx3 : D x3) 
                (xx4 : D x4) 
                (yy : D y) 
                (ff0 : xx3 -->[ f0] xx4),
                let t :=
                  (λ (x y0 : V) 
                   (xx : D x) 
                   (yy0 : D y0), 
                   B x y0 xx yy0) x3 y xx3 yy ;; 
                  (λ (x y3 y4 : V) 
                   (g0 : V ⟦ y3, y4 ⟧) 
                   (xx : D x) 
                   (yy3 : D y3) 
                   (yy4 : D y4)
                   (gg0 : yy3 -->[ g0] yy4),
                   Tmor x y3 y4 g0 xx yy3 yy4 gg0) y
                    x3 x4 f0 yy xx3 xx4 ff0 ;; 
                  (λ (x y0 : V) 
                   (xx : D x)

                 x2 y2 f xx1 xx2 yy2 ff)
 intro ; intros ; apply LP.
  
V: sym_monoidal_cat
D: disp_cat V
LP: locally_propositional D
T: ∏ x y : V, D x → D y → D (x ⊗ y)
Tmor: ∏ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧) 
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) (yy2 : D y2),
yy1 -->[ g] yy2
→ T x y1 xx yy1 -->[
  x ⊗^{ V}_{l} g] T x y2 xx yy2
B: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) (yy : D y),
T x y xx yy -->[
sym_mon_braiding V x y] T y x yy xx
II: D I_{ V}
lu_lu: ∏ (x : V) (xx : D x),
T I_{ V} x II xx -->[ mon_lunitor x] xx
lu_lu_inv: ∏ (x : V) (xx : D x),
xx -->[ mon_linvunitor x] T I_{ V} x II xx
assass: ∏ (x y z : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y) (zz : D z),
T (x ⊗ y) z (T x y xx yy) zz -->[
mon_lassociator x y z] T x 
                        (y ⊗ z) xx
                        (T y z yy zz)
assassinv: ∏ (x y z : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y) (zz : D z),
T x (y ⊗ z) xx (T y z yy zz) -->[
mon_rassociator x y z] T (x ⊗ y) z
                        (T x y xx yy) zz
D I_{ V}
 exact II.

disp_leftunitor_data
  (make_symmetric_monoidal_disp_cat_tensor V D T Tmor
     B
     (λ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
      (yy : D y),
      let X :=
        λ (x0 y0 : V) (f : V ⟦ x0, y0 ⟧) 
        (xx0 : D x0) (yy0 : D y0)
        (x1 x' : xx0 -->[ f] yy0),
        pr1 (LP x0 y0 f xx0 yy0 x1 x') in
      X (x ⊗ y) (x ⊗ y) (x ⊗^{ V}_{l} identity y)
        (T x y xx yy) (T x y xx yy)
        (Tmor x y y (identity y) xx yy yy (id_disp yy))
        (transportb
           (mor_disp (T x y xx yy) (T x y xx yy))
           (bifunctor_leftid V x y)
           (id_disp (T x y xx yy))))
     (λ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
      (yy : D y),
      let X :=
        λ (x0 y0 : V) (f : V ⟦ x0, y0 ⟧) 
        (xx0 : D x0) (yy0 : D y0)
        (x1 x' : xx0 -->[ f] yy0),
        pr1 (LP x0 y0 f xx0 yy0 x1 x') in
      X (x ⊗ y) (x ⊗ y)
        (sym_mon_braiding V x y
         · sym_mon_braiding V y x) 
        (T x y xx yy) (T x y xx yy)
        (B x y xx yy ;; B y x yy xx)
        (transportb
           (mor_disp (T x y xx yy) (T x y xx yy))
           (sym_mon_braiding_inv V x y)
           (id_disp (T x y xx yy))))
     (λ (x y1 y2 y3 : V) 
      (g1 : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧) 
      (g2 : V ⟦ y2, y3 ⟧) 
      (xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
      (yy2 : D y2) (yy3 : D y3)
      (gg1 : yy1 -->[ g1] yy2)
      (gg2 : yy2 -->[ g2] yy3),
      let X :=
        λ (x0 y : V) (f : V ⟦ x0, y ⟧) 
        (xx0 : D x0) (yy : D y)
        (x1 x' : xx0 -->[ f] yy),
        pr1 (LP x0 y f xx0 yy x1 x') in
      X (x ⊗ y1) (x ⊗ y3) 
        (x ⊗^{ V}_{l} (g1 · g2)) 
        (T x y1 xx yy1) (T x y3 xx yy3)
        (Tmor x y1 y3 (g1 · g2) xx yy1 yy3
           (gg1 ;; gg2))
        (transportb
           (mor_disp (T x y1 xx yy1) (T x y3 xx yy3))
           (bifunctor_leftcomp V x y1 y2 y3 g1 g2)
           (Tmor x y1 y2 g1 xx yy1 yy2 gg1 ;; 
            Tmor x y2 y3 g2 xx yy2 yy3 gg2)))
     (λ (x1 x2 y1 y2 : V) 
      (f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧) 
      (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧) 
      (xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2) 
      (yy1 : D y1) (yy2 : D y2) 
      (ff : xx1 -->[ f] xx2) 
      (gg : yy1 -->[ g] yy2),
      let X :=
        λ (x y : V) (f0 : V ⟦ x, y ⟧) 
        (xx : D x) (yy : D y)
        (x0 x' : xx -->[ f0] yy),
        pr1 (LP x y f0 xx yy x0 x') in
      X (x1 ⊗ y1) (x2 ⊗ y2)
        (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y1 · x2 ⊗^{ V}_{l} g)
        (T x1 y1 xx1 yy1) 
        (T x2 y2 xx2 yy2)
        ((let t :=
            B x1 y1 xx1 yy1 ;; 
            Tmor y1 x1 x2 f yy1 xx1 xx2 ff ;; 
            B y1 x2 yy1 xx2 in
          transportf
            (mor_disp (T x1 y1 xx1 yy1)
               (T x2 y1 xx2 yy1))
            (maponpaths_2 compose
               (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V
                  x1 x2 y1 f)
               (sym_mon_braiding V y1 x2) @
             assoc' (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y1) 
               (V x2 y1) 
               (sym_mon_braiding V y1 x2) @
             maponpaths (compose (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y1))
               (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x2 y1)) @
             id_right (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y1)) t) ;; 
         Tmor x2 y1 y2 g xx2 yy1 yy2 gg)
        (transportb
           (mor_disp (T x1 y1 xx1 yy1)
              (T x2 y2 xx2 yy2))
           (bifunctor_equalwhiskers V x1 x2 y1 y2 f g)
           (Tmor x1 y1 y2 g xx1 yy1 yy2 gg ;; 
            (let t :=
               B x1 y2 xx1 yy2 ;; 
               Tmor y2 x1 x2 f yy2 xx1 xx2 ff ;; 
               B y2 x2 yy2 xx2 in
             transportf
               (mor_disp 
                  (T x1 y2 xx1 yy2) 
                  (T x2 y2 xx2 yy2))
               (maponpaths_2 compose
                  (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right
                     V x1 x2 y2 f)
                  (sym_mon_braiding V y2 x2) @
                assoc' (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y2) 
                  (V x2 y2) 
                  (sym_mon_braiding V y2 x2) @
                maponpaths 
                  (compose (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y2))
                  (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x2 y2)) @
                id_right (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y2)) t))))) II

      (gg2 : yy2 -->[ g2] yy3),

 exact lu_lu_inv.

disp_associator_data

     B
     (λ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
      (yy : D y),
      let X :=
        λ (x0 y0 : V) (f : V ⟦ x0, y0 ⟧) 
        (xx0 : D x0) (yy0 : D y0)

      X (x ⊗ y) (x ⊗ y) (x ⊗^{ V}_{l} identity y)

        (transportb
           (mor_disp (T x y xx yy) (T x y xx yy))
           (bifunctor_leftid V x y)
           (id_disp (T x y xx yy))))
     (λ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
      (yy : D y),
      let X :=
        λ (x0 y0 : V) (f : V ⟦ x0, y0 ⟧) 
        (xx0 : D x0) (yy0 : D y0)

        pr1 (LP x0 y0 f xx0 yy0 x1 x') in
      X (x ⊗ y) (x ⊗ y)

        (transportb
           (mor_disp (T x y xx yy) (T x y xx yy))
           (sym_mon_braiding_inv V x y)
           (id_disp (T x y xx yy))))
     (λ (x y1 y2 y3 : V) 
      (g1 : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧) 
      (g2 : V ⟦ y2, y3 ⟧) 
      (xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
      (yy2 : D y2) (yy3 : D y3)
      (gg1 : yy1 -->[ g1] yy2)
      (gg2 : yy2 -->[ g2] yy3),
      let X :=
        λ (x0 y : V) (f : V ⟦ x0, y ⟧) 
        (xx0 : D x0) (yy : D y)
        (x1 x' : xx0 -->[ f] yy),
        pr1 (LP x0 y f xx0 yy x1 x') in
      X (x ⊗ y1) (x ⊗ y3) 
        (x ⊗^{ V}_{l} (g1 · g2))

        (Tmor x y1 y3 (g1 · g2) xx yy1 yy3
           (gg1 ;; gg2))
        (transportb
           (mor_disp (T x y1 xx yy1) (T x y3 xx yy3))
           (bifunctor_leftcomp V x y1 y2 y3 g1 g2)
           (Tmor x y1 y2 g1 xx yy1 yy2 gg1 ;; 
            Tmor x y2 y3 g2 xx yy2 yy3 gg2)))
     (λ (x1 x2 y1 y2 : V) 
      (f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧) 
      (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧) 
      (xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2)

      (gg : yy1 -->[ g] yy2),

      X (x1 ⊗ y1) (x2 ⊗ y2)
        (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y1 · x2 ⊗^{ V}_{l} g)

        (T x2 y2 xx2 yy2)
        ((let t :=
            B x1 y1 xx1 yy1 ;; 
            Tmor y1 x1 x2 f yy1 xx1 xx2 ff ;; 
            B y1 x2 yy1 xx2 in
          transportf
            (mor_disp (T x1 y1 xx1 yy1)
               (T x2 y1 xx2 yy1))
            (maponpaths_2 compose
               (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V
                  x1 x2 y1 f)
               (sym_mon_braiding V y1 x2) @
             assoc' (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y1) 
               (V x2 y1) 
               (sym_mon_braiding V y1 x2) @
             maponpaths (compose (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y1))
               (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x2 y1)) @
             id_right (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y1)) t) ;; 
         Tmor x2 y1 y2 g xx2 yy1 yy2 gg)
        (transportb
           (mor_disp (T x1 y1 xx1 yy1)
              (T x2 y2 xx2 yy2))
           (bifunctor_equalwhiskers V x1 x2 y1 y2 f g)
           (Tmor x1 y1 y2 g xx1 yy1 yy2 gg ;; 
            (let t :=
               B x1 y2 xx1 yy2 ;; 
               Tmor y2 x1 x2 f yy2 xx1 xx2 ff ;; 
               B y2 x2 yy2 xx2 in
             transportf
               (mor_disp 
                  (T x1 y2 xx1 yy2) 
                  (T x2 y2 xx2 yy2))
               (maponpaths_2 compose
                  (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right
                     V x1 x2 y2 f)
                  (sym_mon_braiding V y2 x2) @
                assoc' (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y2) 
                  (V x2 y2) 
                  (sym_mon_braiding V y2 x2) @
                maponpaths 
                  (compose (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y2))
                  (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x2 y2)) @
                id_right (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y2)) t)))))
 exact assass.
  
V: sym_monoidal_cat
D: disp_cat V
LP: locally_propositional D
T: ∏ x y : V, D x → D y → D (x ⊗ y)
Tmor: ∏ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧) 
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) (yy2 : D y2),
yy1 -->[ g] yy2
→ T x y1 xx yy1 -->[
  x ⊗^{ V}_{l} g] T x y2 xx yy2
B: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) (yy : D y),
T x y xx yy -->[
sym_mon_braiding V x y] T y x yy xx
II: D I_{ V}
lu_lu: ∏ (x : V) (xx : D x),
T I_{ V} x II xx -->[ mon_lunitor x] xx
lu_lu_inv: ∏ (x : V) (xx : D x),
xx -->[ mon_linvunitor x] T I_{ V} x II xx
assass: ∏ (x y z : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y) (zz : D z),
T (x ⊗ y) z (T x y xx yy) zz -->[
mon_lassociator x y z] T x 
                        (y ⊗ z) xx
                        (T y z yy zz)
assassinv: ∏ (x y z : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y) (zz : D z),
T x (y ⊗ z) xx (T y z yy zz) -->[
mon_rassociator x y z] T (x ⊗ y) z
                        (T x y xx yy) zz
disp_associatorinv_data
  (make_symmetric_monoidal_disp_cat_tensor V D T Tmor
     B
     (λ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
      (yy : D y),
      let X :=
        λ (x0 y0 : V) (f : V ⟦ x0, y0 ⟧) 
        (xx0 : D x0) (yy0 : D y0)
        (x1 x' : xx0 -->[ f] yy0),
        pr1 (LP x0 y0 f xx0 yy0 x1 x') in
      X (x ⊗ y) (x ⊗ y) (x ⊗^{ V}_{l} identity y)
        (T x y xx yy) (T x y xx yy)
        (Tmor x y y (identity y) xx yy yy (id_disp yy))
        (transportb
           (mor_disp (T x y xx yy) (T x y xx yy))
           (bifunctor_leftid V x y)
           (id_disp (T x y xx yy))))
     (λ (x y : V) (xx : D x) 
      (yy : D y),
      let X :=
        λ (x0 y0 : V) (f : V ⟦ x0, y0 ⟧) 
        (xx0 : D x0) (yy0 : D y0)
        (x1 x' : xx0 -->[ f] yy0),
        pr1 (LP x0 y0 f xx0 yy0 x1 x') in
      X (x ⊗ y) (x ⊗ y)
        (sym_mon_braiding V x y
         · sym_mon_braiding V y x) 
        (T x y xx yy) (T x y xx yy)
        (B x y xx yy ;; B y x yy xx)
        (transportb
           (mor_disp (T x y xx yy) (T x y xx yy))
           (sym_mon_braiding_inv V x y)
           (id_disp (T x y xx yy))))
     (λ (x y1 y2 y3 : V) 
      (g1 : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧) 
      (g2 : V ⟦ y2, y3 ⟧) 
      (xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) 
      (yy2 : D y2) (yy3 : D y3)
      (gg1 : yy1 -->[ g1] yy2)
      (gg2 : yy2 -->[ g2] yy3),
      let X :=
        λ (x0 y : V) (f : V ⟦ x0, y ⟧) 
        (xx0 : D x0) (yy : D y)
        (x1 x' : xx0 -->[ f] yy),
        pr1 (LP x0 y f xx0 yy x1 x') in
      X (x ⊗ y1) (x ⊗ y3) 
        (x ⊗^{ V}_{l} (g1 · g2)) 
        (T x y1 xx yy1) (T x y3 xx yy3)
        (Tmor x y1 y3 (g1 · g2) xx yy1 yy3
           (gg1 ;; gg2))
        (transportb
           (mor_disp (T x y1 xx yy1) (T x y3 xx yy3))
           (bifunctor_leftcomp V x y1 y2 y3 g1 g2)
           (Tmor x y1 y2 g1 xx yy1 yy2 gg1 ;; 
            Tmor x y2 y3 g2 xx yy2 yy3 gg2)))
     (λ (x1 x2 y1 y2 : V) 
      (f : V ⟦ x1, x2 ⟧) 
      (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧) 
      (xx1 : D x1) (xx2 : D x2) 
      (yy1 : D y1) (yy2 : D y2) 
      (ff : xx1 -->[ f] xx2) 
      (gg : yy1 -->[ g] yy2),
      let X :=
        λ (x y : V) (f0 : V ⟦ x, y ⟧) 
        (xx : D x) (yy : D y)
        (x0 x' : xx -->[ f0] yy),
        pr1 (LP x y f0 xx yy x0 x') in
      X (x1 ⊗ y1) (x2 ⊗ y2)
        (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y1 · x2 ⊗^{ V}_{l} g)
        (T x1 y1 xx1 yy1) 
        (T x2 y2 xx2 yy2)
        ((let t :=
            B x1 y1 xx1 yy1 ;; 
            Tmor y1 x1 x2 f yy1 xx1 xx2 ff ;; 
            B y1 x2 yy1 xx2 in
          transportf
            (mor_disp (T x1 y1 xx1 yy1)
               (T x2 y1 xx2 yy1))
            (maponpaths_2 compose
               (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right V
                  x1 x2 y1 f)
               (sym_mon_braiding V y1 x2) @
             assoc' (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y1) 
               (V x2 y1) 
               (sym_mon_braiding V y1 x2) @
             maponpaths (compose (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y1))
               (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x2 y1)) @
             id_right (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y1)) t) ;; 
         Tmor x2 y1 y2 g xx2 yy1 yy2 gg)
        (transportb
           (mor_disp (T x1 y1 xx1 yy1)
              (T x2 y2 xx2 yy2))
           (bifunctor_equalwhiskers V x1 x2 y1 y2 f g)
           (Tmor x1 y1 y2 g xx1 yy1 yy2 gg ;; 
            (let t :=
               B x1 y2 xx1 yy2 ;; 
               Tmor y2 x1 x2 f yy2 xx1 xx2 ff ;; 
               B y2 x2 yy2 xx2 in
             transportf
               (mor_disp 
                  (T x1 y2 xx1 yy2) 
                  (T x2 y2 xx2 yy2))
               (maponpaths_2 compose
                  (monoidal_braiding_naturality_right
                     V x1 x2 y2 f)
                  (sym_mon_braiding V y2 x2) @
                assoc' (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y2) 
                  (V x2 y2) 
                  (sym_mon_braiding V y2 x2) @
                maponpaths 
                  (compose (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y2))
                  (pr1 ((pr122 (pr2 V)) x2 y2)) @
                id_right (f ⊗^{ V}_{r} y2)) t)))))
 exact assassinv.
  
V: sym_monoidal_cat
D: disp_cat V
LP: locally_propositional D
T: ∏ x y : V, D x → D y → D (x ⊗ y)
Tmor: ∏ (x y1 y2 : V) (g : V ⟦ y1, y2 ⟧) 
(xx : D x) (yy1 : D y1) (yy2 : D y2),
yy1 -->[ g] yy2
→ T x y1 xx yy1 -->[
  x ⊗^{ V}_{l} g] T x y2 xx yy2
B: ∏ (x y : V) (xx : D x) (yy : D y),
T x y xx yy -->[
sym_mon_braiding V x y] T y x yy xx
II: D I_{ V}
lu_lu: ∏ (x : V) (xx : D x),
T I_{ V} x II xx -->[ mon_lunitor x] xx
lu_lu_inv: ∏ (x : V) (xx : D x),
xx -->[ mon_linvunitor x] T I_{ V} x II xx
assass: ∏ (x y z : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y) (zz : D z),
T (x ⊗ y) z (T x y xx yy) zz -->[
mon_lassociator x y z] T x 
                        (y ⊗ z) xx
                        (T y z yy zz)
assassinv: ∏ (x y z : V) (xx : D x) 
(yy : D y) (zz : D z),
T x (y ⊗ z) xx (T y z yy zz) -->[
mon_rassociator x y z] T (x ⊗ y) z
                        (T x y xx yy) zz
locally_propositional D
 exact LP.
Defined.
